## 1. Orquestrador de Agentes - Dispatcher e Balanceamento de Carga

### `src/agents/orchestrator/dispatcher.js`

```javascript
const EventEmitter = require('events');
const logger = require('../../utils/logger');
const errorHandler = require('../../utils/error-handler');

class AgentDispatcher extends EventEmitter {
    constructor(config) {
        super();
        this.config = config;
        this.agents = new Map();
        this.taskQueue = [];
        this.runningTasks = new Map();
        this.taskHistory = [];
        this.maxConcurrentTasks = config.maxConcurrentTasks || 10;
        this.taskTimeout = config.taskTimeout || 30000;
        
        logger.info('AgentDispatcher initialized', { maxConcurrentTasks: this.maxConcurrentTasks });
    }

    registerAgent(agentId, agentConfig) {
        const agent = {
            id: agentId,
            config: agentConfig,
            capabilities: agentConfig.capabilities || [],
            currentLoad: 0,
            maxLoad: agentConfig.maxLoad || 5,
            status: 'idle',
            lastUsed: Date.now(),
            metrics: {
                tasksCompleted: 0,
                tasksFailed: 0,
                avgResponseTime: 0,
                totalTokensUsed: 0
            }
        };

        this.agents.set(agentId, agent);
        logger.info(`Agent registered: ${agentId}`, { capabilities: agent.capabilities });
        
        return agent;
    }

    unregisterAgent(agentId) {
        if (this.agents.has(agentId)) {
            const agent = this.agents.get(agentId);
            if (agent.status === 'busy') {
                logger.warn(`Unregistering busy agent: ${agentId}`);
                this.reassignTasks(agentId);
            }
            this.agents.delete(agentId);
            logger.info(`Agent unregistered: ${agentId}`);
        }
    }

    async dispatchTask(task) {
        const taskId = `task_${Date.now()}_${Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9)}`;
        const enrichedTask = {
            ...task,
            id: taskId,
            status: 'pending',
            createdAt: Date.now(),
            assignedAgent: null,
            priority: task.priority || 'normal'
        };

        this.taskQueue.push(enrichedTask);
        logger.debug(`Task queued: ${taskId}`, { type: task.type, priority: enrichedTask.priority });

        // Emit event for monitoring
        this.emit('taskQueued', enrichedTask);

        // Process queue if not at capacity
        this.processQueue();

        // Return task promise
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
            const taskCompleteHandler = (completedTask) => {
                if (completedTask.id === taskId) {
                    this.removeListener('taskCompleted', taskCompleteHandler);
                    this.removeListener('taskFailed', taskFailedHandler);
                    
                    if (completedTask.status === 'completed') {
                        resolve(completedTask.result);
                    } else {
                        reject(new Error(completedTask.error || 'Task failed'));
                    }
                }
            };

            const taskFailedHandler = (failedTask) => {
                if (failedTask.id === taskId) {
                    this.removeListener('taskCompleted', taskCompleteHandler);
                    this.removeListener('taskFailed', taskFailedHandler);
                    reject(new Error(failedTask.error || 'Task failed'));
                }
            };

            this.on('taskCompleted', taskCompleteHandler);
            this.on('taskFailed', taskFailedHandler);

            // Set timeout
            setTimeout(() => {
                this.removeListener('taskCompleted', taskCompleteHandler);
                this.removeListener('taskFailed', taskFailedHandler);
                
                const taskIndex = this.taskQueue.findIndex(t => t.id === taskId);
                if (taskIndex !== -1) {
                    const timedOutTask = this.taskQueue.splice(taskIndex, 1)[0];
                    timedOutTask.status = 'timeout';
                    timedOutTask.error = 'Task timeout exceeded';
                    
                    this.emit('taskFailed', timedOutTask);
                    reject(new Error('Task timeout exceeded'));
                }
            }, this.taskTimeout);
        });
    }

    processQueue() {
        // Check if we can process more tasks
        const availableSlots = this.maxConcurrentTasks - this.runningTasks.size;
        
        if (availableSlots <= 0 || this.taskQueue.length === 0) {
            return;
        }

        // Sort tasks by priority (high -> normal -> low)
        this.taskQueue.sort((a, b) => {
            const priorityOrder = { high: 3, normal: 2, low: 1 };
            return priorityOrder[b.priority] - priorityOrder[a.priority];
        });

        // Process up to available slots
        for (let i = 0; i < Math.min(availableSlots, this.taskQueue.length); i++) {
            const task = this.taskQueue.shift();
            this.executeTask(task);
        }
    }

    async executeTask(task) {
        try {
            // Find suitable agent using load balancer
            const agentId = this.selectAgentForTask(task);
            
            if (!agentId) {
                task.status = 'failed';
                task.error = 'No suitable agent available';
                this.taskQueue.unshift(task); // Put back in queue
                this.emit('taskFailed', task);
                return;
            }

            const agent = this.agents.get(agentId);
            
            // Update agent state
            agent.status = 'busy';
            agent.currentLoad++;
            agent.lastUsed = Date.now();
            
            // Update task
            task.status = 'running';
            task.assignedAgent = agentId;
            task.startedAt = Date.now();
            
            this.runningTasks.set(task.id, task);
            
            logger.info(`Task ${task.id} assigned to agent ${agentId}`, {
                taskType: task.type,
                agentLoad: agent.currentLoad
            });

            this.emit('taskStarted', { task, agent });

            // Execute task (simulated - would call actual agent)
            const result = await this.executeAgentTask(agent, task);
            
            // Update metrics
            const executionTime = Date.now() - task.startedAt;
            agent.metrics.tasksCompleted++;
            agent.metrics.avgResponseTime = 
                (agent.metrics.avgResponseTime * (agent.metrics.tasksCompleted - 1) + executionTime) / 
                agent.metrics.tasksCompleted;
            
            // Update task
            task.status = 'completed';
            task.completedAt = Date.now();
            task.result = result;
            task.executionTime = executionTime;
            
            // Cleanup
            agent.status = 'idle';
            agent.currentLoad--;
            this.runningTasks.delete(task.id);
            this.taskHistory.push(task);
            
            // Trim history if too large
            if (this.taskHistory.length > 1000) {
                this.taskHistory = this.taskHistory.slice(-500);
            }
            
            logger.info(`Task ${task.id} completed`, {
                executionTime,
                agentId
            });

            this.emit('taskCompleted', task);
            this.processQueue(); // Check for more tasks

        } catch (error) {
            logger.error(`Task ${task.id} failed`, error);
            
            const agent = this.agents.get(task.assignedAgent);
            if (agent) {
                agent.status = 'idle';
                agent.currentLoad--;
                agent.metrics.tasksFailed++;
            }
            
            task.status = 'failed';
            task.error = error.message;
            task.completedAt = Date.now();
            
            this.runningTasks.delete(task.id);
            this.taskHistory.push(task);
            
            this.emit('taskFailed', task);
            this.processQueue();
        }
    }

    selectAgentForTask(task) {
        const suitableAgents = [];
        
        for (const [agentId, agent] of this.agents.entries()) {
            // Check if agent has required capabilities
            const hasCapabilities = task.requiredCapabilities?.every(cap => 
                agent.capabilities.includes(cap)
            ) ?? true;
            
            // Check if agent can handle more load
            const hasCapacity = agent.currentLoad < agent.maxLoad;
            
            // Check agent status
            const isAvailable = agent.status === 'idle';
            
            if (hasCapabilities && hasCapacity && isAvailable) {
                suitableAgents.push({
                    agentId,
                    loadScore: agent.currentLoad / agent.maxLoad,
                    lastUsed: agent.lastUsed,
                    successRate: agent.metrics.tasksCompleted / 
                               (agent.metrics.tasksCompleted + agent.metrics.tasksFailed || 1)
                });
            }
        }
        
        if (suitableAgents.length === 0) {
            return null;
        }
        
        // Load balancing strategy: weighted score
        const scoredAgents = suitableAgents.map(agent => {
            // Lower load = better, more recent use = better, higher success rate = better
            const score = 
                (1 - agent.loadScore) * 0.4 + 
                ((Date.now() - agent.lastUsed) / 60000 > 5 ? 0.3 : 0.1) + // Prefer recently used but not too recent
                agent.successRate * 0.3;
            
            return { ...agent, score };
        });
        
        // Select agent with highest score
        scoredAgents.sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score);
        return scoredAgents[0].agentId;
    }

    async executeAgentTask(agent, task) {
        // This would be implemented based on actual agent execution
        // For now, simulate execution
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
            setTimeout(() => {
                if (Math.random() < 0.95) { // 95% success rate simulation
                    resolve({
                        taskId: task.id,
                        agentId: agent.id,
                        output: `Processed ${task.type} task`,
                        metadata: {
                            processedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
                            tokensUsed: Math.floor(Math.random() * 100) + 50
                        }
                    });
                } else {
                    reject(new Error('Simulated agent failure'));
                }
            }, Math.random() * 1000 + 500); // Random delay 500-1500ms
        });
    }

    reassignTasks(agentId) {
        const tasksToReassign = [];
        
        for (const [taskId, task] of this.runningTasks.entries()) {
            if (task.assignedAgent === agentId) {
                tasksToReassign.push(task);
                this.runningTasks.delete(taskId);
            }
        }
        
        // Requeue tasks
        tasksToReassign.forEach(task => {
            task.status = 'pending';
            task.assignedAgent = null;
            this.taskQueue.unshift(task); // High priority for reassigned tasks
        });
        
        if (tasksToReassign.length > 0) {
            logger.warn(`Reassigned ${tasksToReassign.length} tasks from agent ${agentId}`);
        }
    }

    getMetrics() {
        const agentsMetrics = {};
        let totalTasks = 0;
        let completedTasks = 0;
        let failedTasks = 0;
        
        for (const [agentId, agent] of this.agents.entries()) {
            agentsMetrics[agentId] = {
                ...agent.metrics,
                currentLoad: agent.currentLoad,
                status: agent.status,
                capabilities: agent.capabilities
            };
            
            totalTasks += agent.metrics.tasksCompleted + agent.metrics.tasksFailed;
            completedTasks += agent.metrics.tasksCompleted;
            failedTasks += agent.metrics.tasksFailed;
        }
        
        return {
            agents: agentsMetrics,
            queue: {
                pending: this.taskQueue.length,
                running: this.runningTasks.size,
                completed: this.taskHistory.filter(t => t.status === 'completed').length,
                failed: this.taskHistory.filter(t => t.status === 'failed').length
            },
            totals: {
                tasks: totalTasks,
                completed: completedTasks,
                failed: failedTasks,
                successRate: totalTasks > 0 ? (completedTasks / totalTasks) * 100 : 0
            },
            performance: {
                avgQueueTime: this.calculateAverageQueueTime(),
                avgExecutionTime: this.calculateAverageExecutionTime()
            }
        };
    }

    calculateAverageQueueTime() {
        const completedTasks = this.taskHistory.filter(t => t.status === 'completed');
        if (completedTasks.length === 0) return 0;
        
        const totalQueueTime = completedTasks.reduce((sum, task) => {
            return sum + (task.startedAt - task.createdAt);
        }, 0);
        
        return totalQueueTime / completedTasks.length;
    }

    calculateAverageExecutionTime() {
        const completedTasks = this.taskHistory.filter(t => t.status === 'completed');
        if (completedTasks.length === 0) return 0;
        
        const totalExecTime = completedTasks.reduce((sum, task) => {
            return sum + (task.executionTime || 0);
        }, 0);
        
        return totalExecTime / completedTasks.length;
    }

    cleanup() {
        // Cleanup old task history
        const cutoff = Date.now() - (24 * 60 * 60 * 1000); // 24 hours
        this.taskHistory = this.taskHistory.filter(task => task.createdAt > cutoff);
        
        logger.debug('Dispatcher cleanup completed', {
            tasksRemoved: this.taskHistory.length
        });
    }
}

module.exports = AgentDispatcher;
```

### `src/agents/orchestrator/load-balancer.js`

```javascript
const logger = require('../../utils/logger');

class LoadBalancer {
    constructor(strategy = 'weighted') {
        this.strategy = strategy;
        this.agentStats = new Map();
        this.strategies = {
            roundRobin: this.roundRobin.bind(this),
            weighted: this.weighted.bind(this),
            leastConnections: this.leastConnections.bind(this),
            latencyBased: this.latencyBased.bind(this)
        };
    }

    updateAgentStats(agentId, stats) {
        this.agentStats.set(agentId, {
            ...stats,
            lastUpdated: Date.now()
        });
    }

    selectAgent(availableAgents, taskRequirements = {}) {
        if (availableAgents.length === 0) {
            return null;
        }

        if (availableAgents.length === 1) {
            return availableAgents[0];
        }

        const strategyFn = this.strategies[this.strategy] || this.strategies.weighted;
        return strategyFn(availableAgents, taskRequirements);
    }

    roundRobin(availableAgents) {
        // Simple round-robin implementation
        if (!this.lastSelectedIndex || this.lastSelectedIndex >= availableAgents.length - 1) {
            this.lastSelectedIndex = 0;
        } else {
            this.lastSelectedIndex++;
        }
        
        return availableAgents[this.lastSelectedIndex];
    }

    weighted(availableAgents, taskRequirements) {
        const scoredAgents = availableAgents.map(agentId => {
            const stats = this.agentStats.get(agentId) || {};
            
            // Calculate score based on multiple factors
            let score = 100; // Base score
            
            // Factor 1: Current load (lower is better)
            const loadFactor = 1 - (stats.currentLoad / (stats.maxLoad || 5));
            score *= 0.3 + (loadFactor * 0.7);
            
            // Factor 2: Success rate
            const successRate = stats.successRate || 1;
            score *= 0.5 + (successRate * 0.5);
            
            // Factor 3: Response time (faster is better)
            if (stats.avgResponseTime) {
                const responseFactor = Math.max(0, 1 - (stats.avgResponseTime / 5000)); // Normalize to 5 seconds
                score *= 0.7 + (responseFactor * 0.3);
            }
            
            // Factor 4: Capability match
            if (taskRequirements.requiredCapabilities && stats.capabilities) {
                const matchRatio = taskRequirements.requiredCapabilities.filter(cap => 
                    stats.capabilities.includes(cap)
                ).length / taskRequirements.requiredCapabilities.length;
                
                score *= 0.5 + (matchRatio * 0.5);
            }
            
            // Factor 5: Recent failures (penalize)
            if (stats.recentFailures && stats.recentFailures > 0) {
                score *= Math.max(0.1, 1 - (stats.recentFailures * 0.2));
            }
            
            return {
                agentId,
                score
            };
        });
        
        // Select agent with highest score
        scoredAgents.sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score);
        
        logger.debug('Weighted load balancing selection', {
            agents: scoredAgents.map(a => ({ agent: a.agentId, score: Math.round(a.score) })),
            selected: scoredAgents[0]?.agentId
        });
        
        return scoredAgents[0]?.agentId;
    }

    leastConnections(availableAgents) {
        let minConnections = Infinity;
        let selectedAgent = null;
        
        for (const agentId of availableAgents) {
            const stats = this.agentStats.get(agentId);
            const connections = stats?.currentLoad || 0;
            
           

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Análise de Arquitetura e Blueprint

## 1. ANÁLISE TÉCNICA DA BASE V10

### 1.1. Pontos Críticos Identificados

```javascript
// Arquivo: v10_analysis_report.md
# Relatório de Análise Técnica - DIYAPP V10
## Data: 2024-01-15
## Status: Crítico

### 1.1.1 Gargalos de Performance
- **Monolito Acoplado**: Base atual é um único serviço Node.js com 12+ responsabilidades
- **Database Single Point of Failure**: PostgreSQL único sem replicação
- **Cache Inexistente**: Queries repetitivas sem mecanismo de cache
- **Fila Síncrona**: Processamento em lote bloqueante
- **Asset Loading**: Frontend carrega 4.2MB de JS na inicialização

### 1.1.2 Pontos Únicos de Falha (SPOF)
1. **API Gateway Único**: Nginx single instance
2. **Banco de Dados Primário**: PostgreSQL sem standby
3. **Serviço de Autenticação**: JWT validation centralizado
4. **Message Broker**: RabbitMQ single node
5. **Storage de Uploads**: S3-like local sem redundância

### 1.1.3 Débito Técnico Acumulado
- Test coverage: 62% (meta: 85%)
- Dependências desatualizadas: 47 pacotes com vulnerabilidades
- Código duplicado: 23% do codebase
- Documentação de API: 40% desatualizada
```

## 2. ARQUITETURA V11 - BLUEPRINT DE MICROSSERVIÇOS

```yaml
# Arquivo: v11_architecture_blueprint.yaml
version: '3.8'
services:
  # Core Services
  api-gateway:
    image: nginx:alpine
    configs:
      - source: gateway_config
    deploy:
      replicas: 3
      placement:
        constraints:
          - node.role == manager
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "-f", "http://localhost:80/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3

  auth-service:
    build: ./services/auth
    environment:
      - JWT_SECRET=${JWT_SECRET}
      - REDIS_URL=redis://redis-sentinel:26379
    depends_on:
      - postgres-primary
      - redis-sentinel
    deploy:
      replicas: 2
      update_config:
        parallelism: 1
        delay: 10s

  user-service:
    build: ./services/users
    environment:
      - DB_HOST=postgres-primary
      - CACHE_HOST=redis-sentinel
    deploy:
      replicas: 3

  # Async Processing
  task-queue:
    image: rabbitmq:3.11-management
    environment:
      - RABBITMQ_DEFAULT_USER=${RABBITMQ_USER}
      - RABBITMQ_DEFAULT_PASS=${RABBITMQ_PASS}
    volumes:
      - rabbitmq_data:/var/lib/rabbitmq
    deploy:
      mode: replicated
      replicas: 3
      placement:
        constraints:
          - node.labels.queue == true

  worker-service:
    build: ./services/worker
    environment:
      - RABBITMQ_HOST=task-queue
      - CONCURRENCY=5
    deploy:
      replicas: 5
      restart_policy:
        condition: on-failure
        max_attempts: 3

  # Data Layer
  postgres-primary:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    environment:
      - POSTGRES_DB=${DB_NAME}
      - POSTGRES_USER=${DB_USER}
      - POSTGRES_PASSWORD=${DB_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    command: >
      postgres
      -c max_connections=200
      -c shared_buffers=256MB
      -c effective_cache_size=1GB
    deploy:
      placement:
        constraints:
          - node.labels.db == primary

  postgres-replica:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    environment:
      - POSTGRES_DB=${DB_NAME}
      - POSTGRES_USER=${DB_USER}
      - POSTGRES_PASSWORD=${DB_PASSWORD}
    command: >
      postgres
      -c hot_standby=on
    volumes:
      - postgres_replica_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    deploy:
      replicas: 2
      placement:
        constraints:
          - node.labels.db == replica

  redis-sentinel:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    command: redis-sentinel /usr/local/etc/redis/sentinel.conf
    volumes:
      - ./config/redis/sentinel.conf:/usr/local/etc/redis/sentinel.conf
    deploy:
      replicas: 3
      placement:
        constraints:
          - node.labels.cache == true

  # Observability Stack
  prometheus:
    image: prom/prometheus:latest
    volumes:
      - ./config/prometheus.yml:/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml
      - prometheus_data:/prometheus
    command:
      - '--config.file=/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml'
      - '--storage.tsdb.path=/prometheus'
      - '--web.console.libraries=/etc/prometheus/console_libraries'
      - '--web.console.templates=/etc/prometheus/consoles'
      - '--storage.tsdb.retention.time=200h'
      - '--web.enable-lifecycle'
    deploy:
      placement:
        constraints:
          - node.role == manager

  grafana:
    image: grafana/grafana:latest
    environment:
      - GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD=${GRAFANA_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - grafana_data:/var/lib/grafana
      - ./config/grafana/provisioning:/etc/grafana/provisioning
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    deploy:
      placement:
        constraints:
          - node.role == manager

  jaeger:
    image: jaegertracing/all-in-one:latest
    environment:
      - COLLECTOR_ZIPKIN_HOST_PORT=:9411
      - COLLECTOR_OTLP_ENABLED=true
    ports:
      - "16686:16686"
      - "4317:4317"
      - "4318:4318"
      - "9411:9411"
    deploy:
      placement:
        constraints:
          - node.role == manager

  loki:
    image: grafana/loki:latest
    command: -config.file=/etc/loki/local-config.yaml
    volumes:
      - loki_data:/loki
    deploy:
      placement:
        constraints:
          - node.role == manager

volumes:
  postgres_data:
    driver: local
  postgres_replica_data:
    driver: local
  rabbitmq_data:
    driver: local
  prometheus_data:
    driver: local
  grafana_data:
    driver: local
  loki_data:
    driver: local

configs:
  gateway_config:
    file: ./config/nginx/nginx.conf
```

## 3. PADRÕES DE CÓDIGO V11

```typescript
// Arquivo: src/engineering-standards.md
# Engineering Standards - DIYAPP V11

## 3.1. Estrutura de Microsserviço
```
services/
├── auth-service/
│   ├── src/
│   │   ├── controllers/
│   │   ├── services/
│   │   ├── repositories/
│   │   ├── middleware/
│   │   ├── utils/
│   │   └── types/
│   ├── tests/
│   │   ├── unit/
│   │   ├── integration/
│   │   └── e2e/
│   ├── Dockerfile
│   ├── docker-compose.yml
│   ├── package.json
│   └── tsconfig.json
```

## 3.2. Template de Service
```typescript
// Arquivo: services/template-service/src/index.ts
import express from 'express';
import helmet from 'helmet';
import cors from 'cors';
import { createLogger, metricsMiddleware, tracingMiddleware } from '@diyapp/observability';
import { errorHandler, notFoundHandler } from '@diyapp/middleware';
import { connectDatabase } from './config/database';
import { connectCache } from './config/cache';
import { registerRoutes } from './routes';
import { healthCheck } from './health';

const app = express();
const logger = createLogger(process.env.SERVICE_NAME || 'template-service');
const PORT = process.env.PORT || 3000;

// Security middleware
app.use(helmet());
app.use(cors({
  origin: process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS?.split(',') || [],
  credentials: true
}));

// Observability middleware
app.use(metricsMiddleware);
app.use(tracingMiddleware);

// Body parsing
app.use(express.json({ limit: '10mb' }));
app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true }));

// Request logging
app.use((req, res, next) => {
  logger.info(`${req.method} ${req.path}`, {
    ip: req.ip,
    userAgent: req.get('user-agent')
  });
  next();
});

// Routes
app.use('/health', healthCheck);
registerRoutes(app);

// Error handling
app.use(notFoundHandler);
app.use(errorHandler);

// Graceful shutdown
const signals = ['SIGINT', 'SIGTERM'];
signals.forEach(signal => {
  process.on(signal, async () => {
    logger.info(`Received ${signal}, starting graceful shutdown`);
    // Close connections here
    process.exit(0);
  });
});

// Startup
async function start() {
  try {
    await connectDatabase();
    await connectCache();
    
    app.listen(PORT, () => {
      logger.info(`Service started on port ${PORT}`);
    });
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Failed to start service', { error });
    process.exit(1);
  }
}

start();
```

## 3.3. Padrão de Repository com Cache
```typescript
// Arquivo: services/user-service/src/repositories/UserRepository.ts
import { Redis } from 'ioredis';
import { Pool } from 'pg';
import { User } from '../types/User';
import { CacheRepository } from './CacheRepository';

export class UserRepository {
  constructor(
    private db: Pool,
    private cache: Redis,
    private cacheRepo: CacheRepository
  ) {}

  async findById(id: string): Promise<User | null> {
    const cacheKey = `user:${id}`;
    
    // Try cache first
    const cached = await this.cacheRepo.get<User>(cacheKey);
    if (cached) {
      return cached;
    }

    // Database query with circuit breaker
    const result = await this.db.query(
      'SELECT * FROM users WHERE id = $1 AND deleted_at IS NULL',
      [id]
    );

    if (result.rows.length === 0) {
      return null;
    }

    const user = result.rows[0];
    
    // Cache with TTL
    await this.cacheRepo.set(cacheKey, user, 300); // 5 minutes
    
    return user;
  }

  async update(id: string, data: Partial<User>): Promise<User> {
    const fields = Object.keys(data);
    const values = Object.values(data);
    
    const setClause = fields
      .map((field, index) => `${field} = $${index + 2}`)
      .join(', ');
    
    const query = `
      UPDATE users 
      SET ${setClause}, updated_at = NOW() 
      WHERE id = $1 
      RETURNING *
    `;
    
    const result = await this.db.query(query, [id, ...values]);
    const updatedUser = result.rows[0];
    
    // Invalidate cache
    await this.cache.del(`user:${id}`);
    
    // Publish event for eventual consistency
    await this.cache.publish('user:updated', JSON.stringify({
      id,
      event: 'USER_UPDATED',
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    }));
    
    return updatedUser;
  }
}
```

```yaml

  - job_name: 'node-services'
    static_configs:
      - targets: 
        - 'auth-service:3000'
        - 'user-service:3001'
        - 'product-service:3002'
    metrics_path: '/metrics'

  - job_name: 'postgres'
    static_configs:
      - targets: ['postgres-exporter:9187']

  - job_name: 'rabbitmq'
    static_configs:
      - targets: ['rabbitmq-exporter:9419']

  - job_name: 'redis'
    static_configs:
      - targets: ['redis-exporter:9121']
```

```typescript
// Arquivo: packages/observability/src/index.ts
import winston from 'winston';
import { createLogger as createWinstonLogger, format, transports } from 'winston';
import { Counter, Histogram, register } from 'prom-client';
import { trace, context, SpanStatusCode } from '@opentelemetry/api';

// Metrics
export const httpRequestCounter = new Counter({
  name: 'http_requests_total',
  help: 'Total HTTP requests',
  labelNames: ['method', 'route', 'status_code']
});

export const httpRequestDuration = new Histogram({
  name: 'http_request_duration_seconds',
  help: 'HTTP request duration in seconds',
  labelNames: ['method', 'route', 'status_code'],
  buckets: [0.1, 0.5, 1, 2, 5]
});

export const databaseQueryDuration = new Histogram({
  name: 'database_query_duration_seconds',
  help: 'Database query duration in seconds',
  labelNames: ['operation', 'table'],
  buckets: [0.01, 0.05, 0.1, 0.5, 1]
});

// Logging
export function createLogger(serviceName: string) {
  return createWinstonLogger({
    level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
    defaultMeta: { service: serviceName },
    format: format.combine(
      format.timestamp(),
      format.errors({ stack: true }),
      format.json()
    ),
    transports: [
      new transports.Console(),
      new transports.File({ 
        filename: `logs/${serviceName}-error.log`, 
        level: 'error' 
      }),
      new transports.File({ 
        filename: `logs/${serviceName}-combined.log` 
      })
    ]
  });
}

// Middleware
export function metricsMiddleware(req: any, res: any, next: Function) {
  const start = Date.now();
  const route = req.route?.path || req.path;
  
  res.on('finish', () => {
    const duration = (Date.now() - start) / 1000;
    
    httpRequestCounter.inc({
      method: req.method,
      route,
      status_code: res.statusCode
    });
    
    httpRequestDuration.observe({
      method: req.method,
      route,
      status_code: res.statusCode
    }, duration);
  });
  
  next();
}

export function tracingMiddleware(req: any, res: any, next: Function) {
  const tracer = trace.getTracer('http');
  const span = tracer.startSpan(`${req.method} ${req.path}`);
  
  span.setAttributes({
    'http.method': req.method,
    'http.url': req.url,
    'http.route': req.route?.path || req.path,
    'user.id': req.user?.id || 'anonymous'
  });
  
  const ctx = trace.setSpan(context.active(), span);
  context.with(ctx, () => {
    next();
  });
  
  res.on('finish', () => {
    span.setAttribute('http.status_code', res.statusCode);
    span.setStatus({
      code: res.statusCode >= 400 ? SpanStatusCode.ERROR : SpanStatusCode.OK
    });
    span.end();
  });
}
```

## 5. DEFINITION OF DONE TÉCNICO

```markdown
# Arquivo: technical-definition-of-done.md
# Definition of Done Técnico - Sprint V11

## 5.1. Critérios Obrigatórios por PR/Merge

### ✅ Código
- [ ] Segue padrões de estilo definidos no .eslintrc
- [ ] Passa em todos os testes unitários (cobertura ≥ 85%)
- [ ] Testes de integração para chamadas entre serviços
- [ ] Documentação de API atualizada (OpenAPI/Swagger)
- [ ] Nenhuma vulnerabilidade de segurança (npm audit clean)
- [ ] Migrações de banco reversíveis e testadas
- [ ] Tratamento de erros com logging apropriado

### ✅ Performance
- [ ] Latência p95 < 200ms para endpoints críticos
- [ ] Query N+1 identificada e resolvida
- [ ] Cache implementado onde apropriado (TTL configurado)
- [ ] Assets otimizados (bundle size < 500KB inicial)

### ✅ Observabilidade
- [ ] Métricas expostas em /metrics (Prometheus format)
- [ ] Logs estruturados com correlation ID
- [ ] Tracing configurado para operações cross-service
- [ ] Health checks implementados (/health, /ready)

### ✅ Segurança
- [ ] Input validation em todos os endpoints
- [ ] Rate limiting para endpoints públicos
- [ ] Headers de segurança (CSP, HSTS, etc.)
- [ ] Secrets gerenciados via vault/ambiente


### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]

## 2. Utilitários Base

### src/utils/logger.js
```javascript
const winston = require('winston');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');

class Logger {
  constructor() {
    this.logger = winston.createLogger({
      level: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production' ? 'info' : 'debug',
      format: winston.format.combine(
        winston.format.timestamp(),
        winston.format.json()
      ),
      defaultMeta: { service: 'diyapp-v11-core' },
      transports: [
        new winston.transports.File({ 
          filename: 'logs/error.log', 
          level: 'error',
          maxsize: 5242880, // 5MB
          maxFiles: 5
        }),
        new winston.transports.File({ 
          filename: 'logs/combined.log',
          maxsize: 5242880,
          maxFiles: 5
        })
      ]
    });

    if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
      this.logger.add(new winston.transports.Console({
        format: winston.format.combine(
          winston.format.colorize(),
          winston.format.simple()
        )
      }));
    }
  }

  generateCorrelationId() {
    return uuidv4();
  }

  maskSensitiveData(data) {
    if (typeof data !== 'object' || data === null) return data;
    
    const masked = { ...data };
    const sensitiveFields = ['password', 'token', 'secret', 'apiKey', 'jwt', 'authorization', 'creditCard', 'cvv', 'ssn', 'cpf'];
    
    sensitiveFields.forEach(field => {
      if (masked[field]) {
        masked[field] = '***MASKED***';
      }
    });
    
    return masked;
  }

  info(message, meta = {}) {
    const correlationId = meta.correlation_id || this.generateCorrelationId();
    this.logger.info(message, { 
      ...this.maskSensitiveData(meta), 
      correlation_id: correlationId 
    });
  }

  error(message, meta = {}) {
    const correlationId = meta.correlation_id || this.generateCorrelationId();
    this.logger.error(message, { 
      ...this.maskSensitiveData(meta), 
      correlation_id: correlationId 
    });
  }

  warn(message, meta = {}) {
    const correlationId = meta.correlation_id || this.generateCorrelationId();
    this.logger.warn(message, { 
      ...this.maskSensitiveData(meta), 
      correlation_id: correlationId 
    });
  }

  debug(message, meta = {}) {
    if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
      const correlationId = meta.correlation_id || this.generateCorrelationId();
      this.logger.debug(message, { 
        ...this.maskSensitiveData(meta), 
        correlation_id: correlationId 
      });
    }
  }

  logRequest(req, res, duration) {
    const correlationId = req.headers['x-correlation-id'] || this.generateCorrelationId();
    
    this.info('HTTP Request', {
      correlation_id: correlationId,
      user_id: req.user?.id || 'anonymous',
      method: req.method,
      endpoint: req.originalUrl,
      status_code: res.statusCode,
      duration_ms: duration,
      user_agent: req.get('user-agent'),
      ip: req.ip
    });
  }

  logError(error, context = {}) {
    this.error(error.message, {
      ...context,
      stack: error.stack,
      name: error.name
    });
  }
}

module.exports = new Logger();
```

### src/utils/error-handler.js
```javascript
const logger = require('./logger');

class AppError extends Error {
  constructor(message, statusCode, code, details = null) {
    super(message);
    this.statusCode = statusCode;
    this.code = code;
    this.details = details;
    this.isOperational = true;
    Error.captureStackTrace(this, this.constructor);
  }
}

class ValidationError extends AppError {
  constructor(message, details) {
    super(message, 422, 'VALIDATION_ERROR', details);
  }
}

class AuthenticationError extends AppError {
  constructor(message = 'Authentication required') {
    super(message, 401, 'AUTHENTICATION_ERROR');
  }
}

class AuthorizationError extends AppError {
  constructor(message = 'Insufficient permissions') {
    super(message, 403, 'AUTHORIZATION_ERROR');
  }
}

class NotFoundError extends AppError {
  constructor(resource, id) {
    super(`${resource} with id ${id} not found`, 404, 'NOT_FOUND');
  }
}

class RateLimitError extends AppError {
  constructor(message = 'Rate limit exceeded') {
    super(message, 429, 'RATE_LIMIT_EXCEEDED');
  }
}

class CircuitBreakerError extends AppError {
  constructor(service) {
    super(`Service ${service} is temporarily unavailable`, 503, 'CIRCUIT_BREAKER_OPEN');
  }
}

const errorHandler = (err, req, res, next) => {
  const correlationId = req.headers['x-correlation-id'] || logger.generateCorrelationId();
  
  // Log the error
  logger.logError(err, {
    correlation_id: correlationId,
    endpoint: req.originalUrl,
    method: req.method,
    user_id: req.user?.id
  });

  // Set default values
  err.statusCode = err.statusCode || 500;
  err.code = err.code || 'INTERNAL_ERROR';
  err.message = err.message || 'Internal server error';

  // Don't leak stack trace in production
  const response = {
    error: {
      code: err.code,
      message: err.message,
      correlation_id: correlationId
    }
  };

  // Add details for validation errors
  if (err.details) {
    response.error.details = err.details;
  }

  // In development, add stack trace
  if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development') {
    response.error.stack = err.stack;
  }

  res.status(err.statusCode).json(response);
};

module.exports = {
  AppError,
  ValidationError,
  AuthenticationError,
  AuthorizationError,
  NotFoundError,
  RateLimitError,
  CircuitBreakerError,
  errorHandler
};
```

### src/utils/config.js
```javascript
require('dotenv').config();

const config = {
  // Server
  env: process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development',
  port: parseInt(process.env.PORT, 10) || 3000,
  apiVersion: process.env.API_VERSION || 'v1',

  // JWT
  jwt: {
    secret: process.env.JWT_SECRET || 'your-super-secret-jwt-key-change-in-production',
    expiresIn: process.env.JWT_EXPIRES_IN || '24h',
    refreshExpiresIn: process.env.JWT_REFRESH_EXPIRES_IN || '7d'
  },

  // Database
  database: {
    type: process.env.DB_TYPE || 'sqlite',
    host: process.env.DB_HOST || 'localhost',
    port: parseInt(process.env.DB_PORT, 10) || 5432,
    name: process.env.DB_NAME || 'diyapp_v11',
    user: process.env.DB_USER || 'postgres',
    password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD || 'postgres',
    sqlitePath: process.env.SQLITE_PATH || './data/diyapp.db'
  },

  // Redis
  redis: {
    host: process.env.REDIS_HOST || 'localhost',
    port: parseInt(process.env.REDIS_PORT, 10) || 6379,
    password: process.env.REDIS_PASSWORD || '',
    tls: process.env.REDIS_TLS === 'true'
  },

  // RabbitMQ
  rabbitmq: {
    host: process.env.RABBITMQ_HOST || 'localhost',
    port: parseInt(process.env.RABBITMQ_PORT, 10) || 5672,
    user: process.env.RABBITMQ_USER || 'guest',
    password: process.env.RABBITMQ_PASSWORD || 'guest',
    vhost: process.env.RABBITMQ_VHOST || '/'
  },

  // Rate Limiting
  rateLimit: {
    windowMs: parseInt(process.env.RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS, 10) || 900000, // 15 minutes
    maxRequests: parseInt(process.env.RATE_LIMIT_MAX_REQUESTS, 10) || 100
  },

  // Circuit Breaker
  circuitBreaker: {
    timeout: parseInt(process.env.CIRCUIT_BREAKER_TIMEOUT, 10) || 30000,
    threshold: parseInt(process.env.CIRCUIT_BREAKER_THRESHOLD, 10) || 5,
    resetTimeout: parseInt(process.env.CIRCUIT_BREAKER_RESET_TIMEOUT, 10) || 60000
  },

  // Hive Mode
  hive: {
    maxConcurrentAgents: parseInt(process.env.MAX_CONCURRENT_AGENTS, 10) || 10,
    agentTimeoutMs: parseInt(process.env.AGENT_TIMEOUT_MS, 10) || 300000,
    taskRetryAttempts: parseInt(process.env.TASK_RETRY_ATTEMPTS, 10) || 3,
    taskRetryDelayMs: parseInt(process.env.TASK_RETRY_DELAY_MS, 10) || 1000
  },

  // API Timeouts
  timeouts: {
    default: 30000,
    database: 10000,
    externalService: 15000,
    llm: 120000 // LLMs get longer timeout
  }
};

// Validate required config
if (config.env === 'production') {
  if (!config.jwt.secret || config.jwt.secret === 'your-super-secret-jwt-key-change-in-production') {
    throw new Error('JWT_SECRET must be set in production');
  }
}

module.exports = config;
```

## 3. Sistema de Fila (Queue)

### src/queue/redis-client.js
```javascript
const redis = require('redis');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');
const config = require('../utils/config');
const { CircuitBreakerError } = require('../utils/error-handler');

class RedisClient {
  constructor() {
    this.client = null;
    this.isConnected = false;
    this.circuitState = 'CLOSED';
    this.failureCount = 0;
    this.lastFailureTime = null;
  }

  async connect() {
    try {
      if (this.circuitState === 'OPEN') {
        const now = Date.now();
        if (now - this.lastFailureTime > config.circuitBreaker.resetTimeout) {
          this.circuitState = 'HALF_OPEN';
          logger.info('Circuit breaker moving to HALF_OPEN state for Redis');
        } else {
          throw new CircuitBreakerError('Redis');
        }
      }

      this.client = redis.createClient({
        socket: {
          host: config.redis.host,
          port: config.redis.port,
          tls: config.redis.tls
        },
        password: config.redis.password
      });

      this.client.on('error', (err) => {
        logger.error('Redis client error', { error: err.message });
        this.handleFailure();
      });

      this.client.on('connect', () => {
        logger.info('Redis connected successfully');
        this.isConnected = true;
        this.resetCircuit();
      });

      await this.client.connect();
      return this.client;
    } catch (error) {
      this.handleFailure();
      logger.error('Failed to connect to Redis', { error: error.message });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  handleFailure() {
    this.failureCount++;
    this.lastFailureTime = Date.now();
    this.isConnected = false;

    if (this.failureCount >= config.circuitBreaker.threshold) {
      this.circuitState = 'OPEN';
      logger.warn('Circuit breaker OPEN for Redis');
    }

  --z-dropdown: 1000;

  --z-fixed: 1030;

## 2. Component Library - UI Components

**src/components/ui/Button/Button.tsx**
```tsx
import React, { ButtonHTMLAttributes, forwardRef } from 'react';
import { cva, type VariantProps } from 'class-variance-authority';
import { cn } from '../../../utils/helpers';

const buttonVariants = cva(
  'inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md font-medium transition-colors focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-offset-2 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50',
  {
    variants: {
      variant: {
        primary: 'bg-primary-600 text-white hover:bg-primary-700 focus-visible:ring-primary-500',
        secondary: 'bg-neutral-200 text-neutral-900 hover:bg-neutral-300 focus-visible:ring-neutral-500',
        outline: 'border border-neutral-300 bg-transparent hover:bg-neutral-100 focus-visible:ring-neutral-500',
        ghost: 'bg-transparent hover:bg-neutral-100 focus-visible:ring-neutral-500',
        danger: 'bg-error text-white hover:bg-error/90 focus-visible:ring-error',
        success: 'bg-success text-white hover:bg-success/90 focus-visible:ring-success',
      },
      size: {
        sm: 'h-8 px-3 text-sm',
        md: 'h-10 px-4',
        lg: 'h-12 px-6 text-lg',
        icon: 'h-10 w-10',
      },
      fullWidth: {
        true: 'w-full',
      },
    },
    defaultVariants: {
      variant: 'primary',
      size: 'md',
    },
  }
);

export interface ButtonProps
  extends ButtonHTMLAttributes<HTMLButtonElement>,
    VariantProps<typeof buttonVariants> {
  loading?: boolean;
  leftIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  rightIcon?: React.ReactNode;
}

const Button = forwardRef<HTMLButtonElement, ButtonProps>(
  ({ className, variant, size, fullWidth, loading, leftIcon, rightIcon, children, disabled, ...props }, ref) => {
    return (
      <button
        className={cn(buttonVariants({ variant, size, fullWidth, className }))}
        ref={ref}
        disabled={disabled || loading}
        aria-busy={loading}
        {...props}
      >
        {loading && (
          <svg
            className="mr-2 h-4 w-4 animate-spin"
            xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"
            fill="none"
            viewBox="0 0 24 24"
            aria-hidden="true"
          >
            <circle
              className="opacity-25"
              cx="12"
              cy="12"
              r="10"
              stroke="currentColor"
              strokeWidth="4"
            />
            <path
              className="opacity-75"
              fill="currentColor"
              d="M4 12a8 8 0 018-8V0C5.373 0 0 5.373 0 12h4zm2 5.291A7.962 7.962 0 014 12H0c0 3.042 1.135 5.824 3 7.938l3-2.647z"
            />
          </svg>
        )}
        {!loading && leftIcon && <span className="mr-2">{leftIcon}</span>}
        {children}
        {!loading && rightIcon && <span className="ml-2">{rightIcon}</span>}
      </button>
    );
  }
);

Button.displayName = 'Button';

export { Button, buttonVariants };
```

**src/components/ui/Modal/Modal.tsx**
```tsx
import React, { useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
import { createPortal } from 'react-dom';
import { cn } from '../../../utils/helpers';
import { Button } from '../Button';

export interface ModalProps {
  isOpen: boolean;
  onClose: () => void;
  title: string;
  children: React.ReactNode;
  size?: 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg' | 'xl';
  showCloseButton?: boolean;
  footer?: React.ReactNode;
  closeOnOverlayClick?: boolean;
  closeOnEsc?: boolean;
}

const Modal: React.FC<ModalProps> = ({
  isOpen,
  onClose,
  title,
  children,
  size = 'md',
  showCloseButton = true,
  footer,
  closeOnOverlayClick = true,
  closeOnEsc = true,
}) => {
  const modalRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!isOpen) return;

    const handleEscape = (e: KeyboardEvent) => {
      if (e.key === 'Escape' && closeOnEsc) {
        onClose();
      }
    };

    document.addEventListener('keydown', handleEscape);
    document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';

    return () => {
      document.removeEventListener('keydown', handleEscape);
      document.body.style.overflow = 'unset';
    };
  }, [isOpen, onClose, closeOnEsc]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (isOpen && modalRef.current) {
      modalRef.current.focus();
    }
  }, [isOpen]);

  if (!isOpen) return null;

  const sizeClasses = {
    sm: 'max-w-md',
    md: 'max-w-lg',
    lg: 'max-w-2xl',
    xl: 'max-w-4xl',
  };

  const handleOverlayClick = (e: React.MouseEvent) => {
    if (closeOnOverlayClick && e.target === e.currentTarget) {
      onClose();
    }
  };

  return createPortal(
    <div
      className="fixed inset-0 z-modal-backdrop flex items-center justify-center bg-black/50 p-4"
      onClick={handleOverlayClick}
      role="dialog"
      aria-modal="true"
      aria-labelledby="modal-title"
    >
      <div
        ref={modalRef}
        className={cn(
          'relative z-modal w-full rounded-lg bg-white shadow-xl',
          sizeClasses[size]
        )}
        tabIndex={-1}
      >
        {/* Header */}
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between border-b border-neutral-200 p-6">
          <h2 id="modal-title" className="text-xl font-semibold text-neutral-900">
            {title}
          </h2>
          {showCloseButton && (
            <Button
              variant="ghost"
              size="icon"
              onClick={onClose}
              aria-label="Close modal"
              className="ml-4"
            >
              <svg
                className="h-5 w-5"
                fill="none"
                viewBox="0 0 24 24"
                stroke="currentColor"
              >
                <path
                  strokeLinecap="round"
                  strokeLinejoin="round"
                  strokeWidth={2}
                  d="M6 18L18 6M6 6l12 12"
                />
              </svg>
            </Button>
          )}
        </div>

        {/* Content */}
        <div className="max-h-[60vh] overflow-y-auto p-6">{children}</div>

        {/* Footer */}
        {footer && (
          <div className="border-t border-neutral-200 p-

### [Sessão Paralela: AI Ops]

## 2. Serviço de Logger

**src/services/logger.js**
```javascript
const winston = require('winston');
const path = require('path');

class LoggerService {
    constructor() {
        this.logger = winston.createLogger({
            level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
            format: winston.format.combine(
                winston.format.timestamp({
                    format: 'YYYY-MM-DD HH:mm:ss'
                }),
                winston.format.errors({ stack: true }),
                winston.format.splat(),
                winston.format.json()
            ),
            defaultMeta: { service: 'hive-orchestrator' },
            transports: [
                new winston.transports.File({ 
                    filename: path.join(__dirname, '../../logs/error.log'), 
                    level: 'error' 
                }),
                new winston.transports.File({ 
                    filename: path.join(__dirname, '../../logs/combined.log') 
                }),
                new winston.transports.Console({
                    format: winston.format.combine(
                        winston.format.colorize(),
                        winston.format.simple()
                    )
                })
            ]
        });
    }

    log(level, message, meta = {}) {
        this.logger.log(level, message, meta);
    }

    info(message, meta = {}) {
        this.log('info', message, meta);
    }

    error(message, meta = {}) {
        this.log('error', message, meta);
    }

    warn(message, meta = {}) {
        this.log('warn', message, meta);
    }

    debug(message, meta = {}) {
        this.log('debug', message, meta);
    }

    // Método específico para monitoramento de IA
    logAIOperation(operation, data) {
        this.info(`AI_OP: ${operation}`, {
            ...data,
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
            costEstimate: this.estimateCost(data),
            tokensUsed: data.tokens || 0
        });
    }

    estimateCost(data) {
        // Estimativa básica de custo baseada em tokens
        const costPerToken = 0.00002; // $0.02 por 1000 tokens
        const tokens = data.tokens || 0;
        return tokens * costPerToken;
    }
}

module.exports = new LoggerService();
```

## 3. Serviço de Cache de LLM

**src/agents/cache/llm-cache.js**
```javascript
const crypto = require('crypto');
const logger = require('../../services/logger');
const AGENTS_CONFIG = require('../../config/agents-config');

class LLMCache {
    constructor(strategy = 'memory') {
        this.strategy = strategy;
        this.cache = new Map();
        this.stats = {
            hits: 0,
            misses: 0,
            size: 0,
            evictions: 0
        };
        
        // Configurações
        this.ttl = AGENTS_CONFIG.cache.ttl * 1000; // converter para ms
        this.maxSize = AGENTS_CONFIG.cache.maxSize;
        
        // Limpeza periódica de entradas expiradas
        setInterval(() => this.cleanup(), 60000); // A cada minuto
    }

    generateKey(prompt, model, parameters = {}) {
        // Gera uma chave única baseada no prompt, modelo e parâmetros
        const content = JSON.stringify({
            prompt: prompt.substring(0, 500), // Limitar tamanho para eficiência
            model,
            temperature: parameters.temperature || 0.7,
            maxTokens: parameters.maxTokens || 1000
        });
        
        return crypto.createHash('sha256').update(content).digest('hex');
    }

    async get(key) {
        const entry = this.cache.get(key);
        
        if (!entry) {
            this.stats.misses++;
            logger.debug('Cache miss', { key });
            return null;
        }

        if (Date.now() > entry.expiresAt) {
            this.cache.delete(key);
            this.stats.size--;
            this.stats.misses++;
            logger.debug('Cache entry expired', { key });
            return null;
        }

        this.stats.hits++;
        logger.debug('Cache hit', { 
            key, 
            tokens: entry.tokens,
            latency: entry.latency 
        });
        
        return entry.data;
    }

    async set(key, data, metadata = {}) {
        // Aplicar política LRU se cache estiver cheio
        if (this.cache.size >= this.maxSize) {
            this.evictLRU();
        }

        const entry = {
            data,
            expiresAt: Date.now() + this.ttl,
            createdAt: Date.now(),
            accessedAt: Date.now(),
            tokens: metadata.tokens || 0,
            latency: metadata.latency || 0,
            model: metadata.model,
            cost: this.calculateCost(metadata.tokens, metadata.model)
        };

        this.cache.set(key, entry);
        this.stats.size++;
        
        logger.info('Cache entry added', {
            key,
            tokens: entry.tokens,
            cost: entry.cost,
            ttl: this.ttl
        });

        return true;
    }

    calculateCost(tokens, model) {
        // Tabela de custos por 1000 tokens
        const costTable = {
            'gpt-4-turbo': 0.01,
            'gpt-3.5-turbo': 0.001,
            'claude-3-opus': 0.015,
            'claude-3-sonnet': 0.003
        };
        
        const costPerToken = (costTable[model] || 0.01) / 1000;
        return tokens * costPerToken;
    }

    evictLRU() {
        let lruKey = null;
        let lruTime = Date.now();

        for (const [key, entry] of this.cache.entries()) {
            if (entry.accessedAt < lruTime) {
                lruTime = entry.accessedAt;
                lruKey = key;
            }
        }

        if (lruKey) {
            this.cache.delete(lruKey);
            this.stats.size--;
            this.stats.evictions++;
            logger.debug('LRU eviction', { key: lruKey });
        }
    }

    cleanup() {
        const now = Date.now();
        let cleaned = 0;

        for (const [key, entry] of this.cache.entries()) {
            if (now > entry.expiresAt) {
                this.cache.delete(key);
                this.stats.size--;
                cleaned++;
            }
        }

        if (cleaned > 0) {
            logger.debug('Cache cleanup completed', { cleaned });
        }
    }

    getStats() {
        return {
            ...this.stats,
            hitRate: this.stats.hits / (this.stats.hits + this.stats.misses) || 0,
            currentSize: this.cache.size,
            maxSize: this.maxSize,
            memoryUsage: process.memoryUsage().heapUsed / 1024 / 1024 // MB
        };
    }

    clear() {
        this.cache.clear();
        this.stats.size = 0;
        logger.info('Cache cleared');
    }
}

module.exports = LLMCache;
```

## 4. Dispatcher de Tarefas

**src/agents/orchestrator/dispatcher.js**
```javascript
const logger = require('../../services/logger');
const TaskManager = require('./task-manager');
const LoadBalancer = require('./load-balancer');
const Validator = require('./validator');

class TaskDispatcher {
    constructor() {
        this.taskManager = new TaskManager();
        this.loadBalancer = new LoadBalancer();
        this.validator = new Validator();
        this.activeTasks = new Map();
        this.taskQueue = [];
        this.maxQueueSize = 1000;
        
        // Métricas
        this.metrics = {
            tasksDispatched: 0,
            tasksCompleted: 0,
            tasksFailed: 0,
            averageLatency: 0,
            queueLength: 0
        };
    }

    async dispatchTask(task) {
        // Validação básica da tarefa
        if (!this.validateTaskStructure(task)) {
            throw new Error('Estrutura de tarefa inválida');
        }

        const taskId = `task-${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9)}`;
        
        const enrichedTask = {
            ...task,
            taskId,
            createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
            status: 'pending',
            retryCount: 0
        };

        // Adicionar à fila se todos os agentes estiverem ocupados
        if (this.loadBalancer.allAgentsBusy()) {
            if (this.taskQueue.length >= this.maxQueueSize) {
                throw new Error('Fila de tarefas cheia');
            }
            
            this.taskQueue.push(enrichedTask);
            this.metrics.queueLength = this.taskQueue.length;
            
            logger.warn('Task queued due to busy agents', {
                taskId,
                queuePosition: this.taskQueue.length,
                estimatedWaitTime: this.estimateWaitTime()
            });
            
            return {
                taskId,
                status: 'queued',
                position: this.taskQueue.length,
                estimatedWaitTime: this.estimateWaitTime()
            };
        }

        // Disparar imediatamente
        return this.executeTask(enrichedTask);
    }

    async executeTask(task) {
        try {
            // Selecionar agente com balanceamento de carga
            const agent = this.loadBalancer.selectAgent(task);
            
            if (!agent) {
                throw new Error('Nenhum agente disponível para a tarefa');
            }

            // Registrar tarefa como ativa
            this.activeTasks.set(task.taskId, {
                task,
                agent,
                startTime: Date.now(),
                status: 'processing'
            });

            this.metrics.tasksDispatched++;
            this.loadBalancer.incrementAgentLoad(agent.id);

            logger.info('Task dispatched', {
                taskId: task.taskId,
                agentId: agent.id,
                taskType: task.type,
                capabilities: task.requiredCapabilities
            });

            // Executar tarefa (simulação - na prática chamaria o agente)
            const result = await this.executeOnAgent(agent, task);

            // Validar resultado
            const validation = this.validator.validateResult(result, task);
            
            if (!validation.valid) {
                throw new Error(`Validação falhou: ${validation.errors.join(', ')}`);
            }

            // Atualizar métricas
            this.completeTask(task.taskId, result);
            
            return {
                taskId: task.taskId,
                status: 'completed',
                result: validation.cleanedResult,
                metrics: {
                    processingTime: Date.now() - this.activeTasks.get(task.taskId).startTime,
                    agentId: agent.id,
                    tokensUsed: result.tokens || 0
                }
            };

        } catch (error) {
            this.failTask(task.taskId, error);
            
            // Tentar retry se aplicável
            if (task.retryCount < 3) {
                task.retryCount++;
                logger.warn('Retrying task', {
                    taskId: task.taskId,
                    retryCount: task.retryCount,
                    error: error.message
                });
                
                return this.executeTask(task);
            }
            
            throw error;
        }
    }

    async executeOnAgent(agent, task) {
        // Simulação de execução no agente
        // Na implementação real, isso chamaria o serviço do agente
        
        return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
            const processingTime = 100 + Math.random() * 400; // 100-500ms
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                // Simular resultado
                const result = {
                    taskId: task.taskId,
                    agentId: agent.id,
                    result: this.generateMockResult(task),
                    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
                    tokens: Math.floor(50 + Math.random() * 200),
                    latency: processingTime
                };
                
                resolve(result);
            }, processingTime);
        });
    }

    generateMockResult(task) {
        // Gerar resultado mock baseado no tipo de tarefa
        switch (task.type) {
            case 'code-refactor':
                return {
                    refactoredCode: '// Código refatorado\nconst x = 10;',
                    changes: ['Renomeou variáveis', 'Extraiu função'],
                    complexityReduction: '15%'
                };
            case 'code-review':
                return {
                    issues: ['Variável não utilizada', 'Complexidade ciclomática alta'],
                    suggestions: ['Extrair função', 'Adicionar tratamento de erro'],
                    score: 85
                };
            default:
                return { completed: true, taskType: task.type };
        }
    }

    completeTask(taskId, result) {
        const taskInfo = this.activeTasks.get(taskId);
        if (!taskInfo) return;

        const processingTime = Date.now() - taskInfo.startTime;
        
        // Atualizar métricas
        this.metrics.tasksCompleted++;
        this.metrics.averageLatency = 
            (this.metrics.averageLatency * (this.metrics.tasksCompleted - 1) + processingTime) / 
            this.metrics.tasksCompleted;
        
        // Liberar agente
        this.loadBalancer.decrementAgentLoad(taskInfo.agent.id);
        
        // Remover tarefa ativa
        this.activeTasks.delete(taskId);
        
        logger.info('Task completed', {
            taskId,
            agentId: taskInfo.agent.id,
            processingTime,
            tokensUsed: result.tokens || 0
        });

        // Processar próxima tarefa da fila
        this.processNextQueuedTask();
    }

    failTask(taskId, error) {
        const taskInfo = this.activeTasks.get(taskId);
        if (!taskInfo) return;

        this.metrics.tasksFailed++;
        this.loadBalancer.decrementAgentLoad(taskInfo.agent.id);
        this.activeTasks.delete(taskId);
        
        logger.error('Task failed', {
            taskId,
            agentId: taskInfo.agent.id,
            error: error.message,
            stack: error.stack
        });
    }

    processNextQueuedTask() {
        if (this.taskQueue.length > 0 && !this.loadBalancer.allAgentsBusy()) {
            const nextTask = this.taskQueue.shift();
            this.metrics.queue

### [Sessão Paralela: SRE]

## 1. Terraform - Provisionamento AWS EKS

### `terraform/main.tf`

```hcl
terraform {
  required_version = ">= 1.5.0"
  required_providers {
    aws = {
      source  = "hashicorp/aws"
      version = "~> 5.0"
    }
    kubernetes = {
      source  = "hashicorp/kubernetes"
      version = "~> 2.23"
    }
    helm = {
      source  = "hashicorp/helm"
      version = "~> 2.11"
    }
  }
  backend "s3" {
    bucket         = "diyapp-v11-terraform-state"
    key            = "prod/terraform.tfstate"
    region         = "us-east-1"
    encrypt        = true
    dynamodb_table = "diyapp-terraform-locks"
  }
}

provider "aws" {
  region = var.aws_region
  default_tags {
    tags = {
      Project     = "DIYAPP-V11"
      Environment = var.environment
      ManagedBy   = "Terraform"
      Squad       = "Autonomous-SRE"
    }
  }
}

# Módulo de rede VPC
module "vpc" {
  source = "./modules/networking"

  environment = var.environment
  vpc_cidr    = var.vpc_cidr
  azs         = var.availability_zones
}

# Módulo EKS Cluster
module "eks_cluster" {
  source = "./modules/eks-cluster"

  cluster_name    = "diyapp-v11-${var.environment}"
  cluster_version = "1.28"
  vpc_id          = module.vpc.vpc_id
  subnet_ids      = module.vpc.private_subnets
  node_groups = {
    main = {
      desired_size   = 3
      max_size       = 10
      min_size       = 3
      instance_types = ["t3.large", "t3a.large"]
      disk_size      = 50
    }
    spot = {
      desired_size   = 2
      max_size       = 6
      min_size       = 2
      instance_types = ["t3.large", "t3a.large", "t3.medium"]
      disk_size      = 50
      spot           = true
    }
  }
  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
  }
}

# Módulo RDS PostgreSQL
module "database" {
  source = "./modules/database"

  environment       = var.environment
  vpc_id            = module.vpc.vpc_id
  subnet_ids        = module.vpc.private_subnets
  db_name           = "diyapp_v11"
  db_username       = var.db_username
  db_password       = var.db_password
  instance_class    = var.environment == "prod" ? "db.t3.large" : "db.t3.medium"
  allocated_storage = var.environment == "prod" ? 100 : 50
  backup_retention_period = var.environment == "prod" ? 30 : 7
}

# Módulo de Monitoramento
module "monitoring" {
  source = "./modules/monitoring"

  environment      = var.environment
  cluster_name     = module.eks_cluster.cluster_name
  cluster_endpoint = module.eks_cluster.cluster_endpoint
  vpc_id           = module.vpc.vpc_id
  subnet_ids       = module.vpc.private_subnets
}

# Configuração do Kubernetes Provider
provider "kubernetes" {
  host                   = module.eks_cluster.cluster_endpoint
  cluster_ca_certificate = base64decode(module.eks_cluster.cluster_certificate_authority_data)
  token                  = data.aws_eks_cluster_auth.cluster.token
}

provider "helm" {
  kubernetes {
    host                   = module.eks_cluster.cluster_endpoint
    cluster_ca_certificate = base64decode(module.eks_cluster.cluster_certificate_authority_data)
    token                  = data.aws_eks_cluster_auth.cluster.token
  }
}

data "aws_eks_cluster_auth" "cluster" {
  name = module.eks_cluster.cluster_name
}

# Configuração de Auto-scaling baseado em métricas
resource "aws_autoscaling_policy" "eks_node_scaling" {
  for_each = module.eks_cluster.node_group_names

  name                   = "diyapp-${var.environment}-${each.value}-scaling"
  autoscaling_group_name = module.eks_cluster.node_group_autoscaling_groups[each.value]
  policy_type            = "TargetTrackingScaling"

  target_tracking_configuration {
    predefined_metric_specification {
      predefined_metric_type = "ASGAverageCPUUtilization"
    }
    target_value = 70.0
  }
}

# CloudWatch Logs para EKS
resource "aws_cloudwatch_log_group" "eks_cluster" {
  name              = "/aws/eks/diyapp-v11-${var.environment}/cluster"
  retention_in_days = var.environment == "prod" ? 90 : 30
}
```

### `terraform/modules/eks-cluster/main.tf`

```hcl
resource "aws_eks_cluster" "main" {
  name     = var.cluster_name
  role_arn = aws_iam_role.cluster.arn
  version  = var.cluster_version

  vpc_config {
    subnet_ids              = var.subnet_ids
    endpoint_private_access = true
    endpoint_public_access  = true
    public_access_cidrs     = ["0.0.0.0/0"]
  }

  enabled_cluster_log_types = ["api", "audit", "authenticator", "controllerManager", "scheduler"]

  tags = var.tags
}

resource "aws_eks_node_group" "groups" {
  for_each = var.node_groups

  cluster_name    = aws_eks_cluster.main.name
  node_group_name = "${var.cluster_name}-${each.key}"
  node_role_arn   = aws_iam_role.nodes.arn
  subnet_ids      = var.subnet_ids

  scaling_config {
    desired_size = each.value.desired_size
    max_size     = each.value.max_size
    min_size     = each.value.min_size
  }

  instance_types = each.value.instance_types
  disk_size      = each.value.disk_size

  capacity_type = each.value.spot ? "SPOT" : "ON_DEMAND"

  tags = merge(var.tags, {
    Name = "${var.cluster_name}-${each.key}"
  })

  depends_on = [
    aws_iam_role_policy_attachment.nodes_AmazonEKSWorkerNodePolicy,
    aws_iam_role_policy_attachment.nodes_AmazonEKS_CNI_Policy,
    aws_iam_role_policy_attachment.nodes_AmazonEC2ContainerRegistryReadOnly,
  ]
}
```

### `terraform/modules/monitoring/main.tf`

```hcl
# Prometheus Server
resource "aws_instance" "prometheus" {
  ami           = data.aws_ami.ubuntu.id
  instance_type = "t3.medium"
  subnet_id     = var.subnet_ids[0]
  vpc_security_group_ids = [aws_security_group.monitoring.id]

  user_data = templatefile("${path.module}/templates/prometheus-setup.sh", {
    cluster_name = var.cluster_name
    environment  = var.environment
  })

  tags = merge(var.tags, {
    Name = "prometheus-${var.environment}"
  })
}

# Grafana Server
resource "aws_instance" "grafana" {
  ami           = data.aws_ami.ubuntu.id
  instance_type = "t3.small"
  subnet_id     = var.subnet_ids[0]
  vpc_security_group_ids = [aws_security_group.monitoring.id]

  user_data = templatefile("${path.module}/templates/grafana-setup.sh", {
    prometheus_endpoint = aws_instance.prometheus.private_ip
    environment         = var.environment
  })

  tags = merge(var.tags, {
    Name = "grafana-${var.environment}"
  })
}

# ELK Stack
resource "aws_elasticsearch_domain" "logs" {
  domain_name           = "diyapp-logs-${var.environment}"
  elasticsearch_version = "7.10"

  cluster_config {
    instance_type          = var.environment == "prod" ? "r6g.large.elasticsearch" : "t3.small.elasticsearch"
    instance_count         = var.environment == "prod" ? 3 : 1
    zone_awareness_enabled = var.environment == "prod"
  }

  ebs_options {
    ebs_enabled = true
    volume_size = var.environment == "prod" ? 100 : 20
  }

  vpc_options {
    subnet_ids         = [var.subnet_ids[0]]
    security_group_ids = [aws_security_group.monitoring.id]
  }

  tags = var.tags
}
```

## 2. Kubernetes Manifests com Health Checks

### `kubernetes/manifests/api-deployment.yaml`

```yaml
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: diyapp-api
  namespace: diyapp
  labels:
    app: diyapp-api
    version: v11
    squad: autonomous-sre
spec:
  replicas: 3
  strategy:
    type: RollingUpdate
    rollingUpdate:
      maxSurge: 1
      maxUnavailable: 0
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: diyapp-api
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: diyapp-api
        version: v11
      annotations:
        prometheus.io/scrape: "true"
        prometheus.io/port: "3000"
        prometheus.io/path: "/metrics"
    spec:
      containers:
      - name: api
        image: ${IMAGE_TAG}
        imagePullPolicy: Always
        ports:
        - containerPort: 3000
          name: http
        env:
        - name: NODE_ENV
          value: "production"
        - name: DATABASE_URL
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              name: database-secret
              key: url
        - name: REDIS_URL
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              name: redis-secret
              key: url
        resources:
          requests:
            memory: "256Mi"
            cpu: "250m"
          limits:
            memory: "512Mi"
            cpu: "500m"
        # Health Checks SLO-based
        livenessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /health/live
            port: 3000
            httpHeaders:
            - name: X-Health-Check
              value: "liveness"
          initialDelaySeconds: 30
          periodSeconds: 10
          timeoutSeconds: 5
          failureThreshold: 3
          successThreshold: 1
        readinessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /health/ready
            port: 3000
            httpHeaders:
            - name: X-Health-Check
              value: "readiness"
          initialDelaySeconds: 5
          periodSeconds: 5
          timeoutSeconds: 3
          failureThreshold: 1
          successThreshold: 1
        startupProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /health/startup
            port: 3000
          initialDelaySeconds: 0
          periodSeconds: 5
          timeoutSeconds: 3
          failureThreshold: 30  # 150s máximo para startup
        # SLO Metrics Exporter
        command: ["node"]
        args:
        - "--require"
        - "@opentelemetry/auto-instrumentations-node/register"
        - "dist/index.js"
---
apiVersion: autoscaling/v2
kind: HorizontalPodAutoscaler
metadata:
  name: diyapp-api-hpa
  namespace: diyapp
spec:
  scaleTargetRef:
    apiVersion: apps/v1
    kind: Deployment
    name: diyapp-api
  minReplicas: 3
  maxReplicas: 10
  metrics:
  - type: Resource
    resource:
      name: cpu
      target:
        type: Utilization
        averageUtilization: 70
  - type: Resource
    resource:
      name: memory
      target:
        type: Utilization
        averageUtilization: 80
  - type: Pods
    pods:
      metric:
        name: http_request_duration_seconds
      target:
        type: AverageValue
        averageValue: 300ms  # SLO Latência P95
  behavior:
    scaleUp:
      stabilizationWindowSeconds: 60
      policies:
      - type: Percent
        value: 100
        periodSeconds: 60
    scaleDown:
      stabilizationWindowSeconds: 300
      policies:
      - type: Percent
        value: 10
        periodSeconds: 60
---
apiVersion: v1
kind: Service
metadata:
  name: diyapp-api
  namespace: diyapp
  annotations:
    prometheus.io/scrape: "true"
    prometheus.io/port: "3000"
spec:
  selector:
    app: diyapp-api
  ports:
  - port: 80
    targetPort: 3000
    name: http
  type: ClusterIP
---
apiVersion: networking.k8s.io/v1
kind: Ingress
metadata:
  name: diyapp-api-ingress
  namespace: diyapp
  annotations:
    kubernetes.io/ingress.class: "alb"
    alb.ingress.kubernetes.io/scheme: "internet-facing"
    alb.ingress.kubernetes.io/target-type: "ip"
    alb.ingress.kubernetes.io/healthcheck-path: "/health/ready"
    alb.ingress.kubernetes.io/healthcheck-interval-seconds: "30"
    alb.ingress.kubernetes.io/healthcheck-timeout-seconds: "5"
    alb.ingress.kubernetes.io/success-codes: "200"
    alb.ingress.kubernetes.io/healthy-threshold-count: "2"
    alb.ingress.kubernetes.io/unhealthy-threshold-count: "2"
spec:
  rules:
  - http:
      paths:
      - path: /
        pathType: Prefix
        backend:
          service:
            name: diyapp-api
            port:
              number: 80
```

### `kubernetes/manifests/monitoring/prometheus-config.yaml`

```yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: ConfigMap
metadata:
  name: prometheus-config
  namespace: monitoring
data:
  prometheus.yml: |
    global:
      scrape_interval: 30s
      evaluation_interval: 30s
      external_labels:
        cluster: 'diyapp-v11'
        environment: '${ENVIRONMENT}'
    
    # SLO Rules Baseadas em Error Budget
    rule_files:
      - /etc/prometheus/rules/slo-rules.yml
    
    scrape_configs:
      - job_name: 'kubernetes-pods'
        kubernetes_sd_configs:
          - role: pod
        relabel_configs:
          - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_pod_annotation_prometheus_io_scrape]
            action: keep
            regex: true
          - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_pod_annotation_prometheus_io_path]
            action: replace
            target_label: __metrics_path__
            regex: (.+)
          - source_labels: [__address__, __meta_kubernetes_pod_annotation_prometheus_io_port]
            action: replace
            regex: ([^:]+)(?::\d+)?;(\d+)
            replacement: $1:$2
            target_label: __address__
          - action: labelmap
            regex: __meta_kubernetes_pod_label_(.+)
          - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_namespace]
            action: replace
            target_label: namespace
          - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_pod_name]
            action: replace
            target_label: pod_name
      
      - job_name: 'kubernetes-apiservers'
        kubernetes_sd_configs:
          - role: endpoints
        scheme: https
        tls_config:
          ca_file: /var/run/secrets/kubernetes.io/serviceaccount/ca.crt
        bearer_token_file: /var/run/secrets/kubernetes.io/serviceaccount/token
        relabel_configs:
          - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_namespace, __meta_kubernetes_service_name, __meta_kubernetes_endpoint_port_name]
            action: keep
            regex: default;kubernetes;https
      
      # SLI Scraping para SLOs
      - job_name: 'sli-availability'
        metrics_path: '/health/ready'
        static_configs:
          - targets:
            - 'diyapp-api.d
