## 1. Schema do Data Lake (BigQuery)

### `src/data_lake/schema_definitions.py`

```python
"""
Schema definitions for DIYAPP Data Lake V11
Following the medallion architecture: Bronze -> Silver -> Gold
"""

from datetime import datetime
from typing import Optional, Dict, List, Any
from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from enum import Enum


class AgentType(Enum):
    """Types of AI agents in the system"""
    DATA_ENGINEER = "data_engineer"
    PRODUCT_MANAGER = "product_manager"
    AI_ENGINEER = "ai_engineer"
    LLM_SPECIALIST = "llm_specialist"
    SRE = "site_reliability_engineer"
    COMPLIANCE = "compliance_officer"


class ExecutionStatus(Enum):
    """Execution status for agent tasks"""
    SUCCESS = "success"
    FAILED = "failed"
    RUNNING = "running"
    PENDING = "pending"
    CANCELLED = "cancelled"


class TelemetryEventType(Enum):
    """Types of telemetry events"""
    AGENT_START = "agent_start"
    AGENT_COMPLETE = "agent_complete"
    AGENT_ERROR = "agent_error"
    USER_INTERACTION = "user_interaction"
    SYSTEM_EVENT = "system_event"
    PERFORMANCE_METRIC = "performance_metric"


@dataclass
class BronzeTelemetry:
    """Raw telemetry data (Bronze layer)"""
    event_id: str
    event_type: str
    agent_id: str
    agent_type: str
    session_id: str
    timestamp: datetime
    raw_data: Dict[str, Any]
    source_system: str
    ingestion_timestamp: datetime = field(default_factory=datetime.utcnow)
    
    @classmethod
    def get_bigquery_schema(cls) -> List[Dict[str, str]]:
        return [
            {"name": "event_id", "type": "STRING", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "event_type", "type": "STRING", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "agent_id", "type": "STRING", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "agent_type", "type": "STRING", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "session_id", "type": "STRING", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "timestamp", "type": "TIMESTAMP", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "raw_data", "type": "STRING", "mode": "REQUIRED"},  # JSON string
            {"name": "source_system", "type": "STRING", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "ingestion_timestamp", "type": "TIMESTAMP", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "partition_date", "type": "DATE", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
        ]


@dataclass
class BronzeAgentPerformance:
    """Raw agent performance metrics (Bronze layer)"""
    metric_id: str
    agent_id: str
    agent_type: str
    task_id: str
    metric_name: str
    metric_value: float
    metric_unit: str
    timestamp: datetime
    context: Dict[str, Any]
    raw_metadata: Dict[str, Any]
    
    @classmethod
    def get_bigquery_schema(cls) -> List[Dict[str, str]]:
        return [
            {"name": "metric_id", "type": "STRING", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "agent_id", "type": "STRING", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "agent_type", "type": "STRING", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "task_id", "type": "STRING", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "metric_name", "type": "STRING", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "metric_value", "type": "FLOAT64", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "metric_unit", "type": "STRING", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "timestamp", "type": "TIMESTAMP", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "context", "type": "STRING", "mode": "REQUIRED"},  # JSON string
            {"name": "raw_metadata", "type": "STRING", "mode": "REQUIRED"},  # JSON string
            {"name": "ingestion_timestamp", "type": "TIMESTAMP", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "partition_date", "type": "DATE", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
        ]


@dataclass
class BronzeExecutionLog:
    """Raw execution logs (Bronze layer)"""
    log_id: str
    execution_id: str
    agent_id: str
    log_level: str
    message: str
    component: str
    timestamp: datetime
    stack_trace: Optional[str]
    metadata: Dict[str, Any]
    
    @classmethod
    def get_bigquery_schema(cls) -> List[Dict[str, str]]:
        return [
            {"name": "log_id", "type": "STRING", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "execution_id", "type": "STRING", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "agent_id", "type": "STRING", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "log_level", "type": "STRING", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "message", "type": "STRING", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "component", "type": "STRING", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "timestamp", "type": "TIMESTAMP", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "stack_trace", "type": "STRING", "mode": "NULLABLE"},
            {"name": "metadata", "type": "STRING", "mode": "REQUIRED"},  # JSON string
            {"name": "ingestion_timestamp", "type": "TIMESTAMP", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "partition_date", "type": "DATE", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
        ]


@dataclass
class SilverTelemetry:
    """Cleaned and standardized telemetry (Silver layer)"""
    event_id: str
    event_type: TelemetryEventType
    agent_id: str
    agent_type: AgentType
    session_id: str
    timestamp: datetime
    duration_ms: Optional[int]
    success: bool
    error_code: Optional[str]
    error_message: Optional[str]
    user_id: Optional[str]
    feature_name: Optional[str]
    processed_data: Dict[str, Any]
    source_system: str
    
    @classmethod
    def get_bigquery_schema(cls) -> List[Dict[str, str]]:
        return [
            {"name": "event_id", "type": "STRING", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "event_type", "type": "STRING", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "agent_id", "type": "STRING", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "agent_type", "type": "STRING", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "session_id", "type": "STRING", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "timestamp", "type": "TIMESTAMP", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "duration_ms", "type": "INT64", "mode": "NULLABLE"},
            {"name": "success", "type": "BOOL", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "error_code", "type": "STRING", "mode": "NULLABLE"},
            {"name": "error_message", "type": "STRING", "mode": "NULLABLE"},
            {"name": "user_id", "type": "STRING", "mode": "NULLABLE"},
            {"name": "feature_name", "type": "STRING", "mode": "NULLABLE"},

            {"name": "agent_id", "type": "STRING", "mode": "REQUIRED"},
            {"name": "agent_type", "type": "STRING", "mode": "REQUIRED"},

```python
"""
Telemetry collector for DIYAPP agents
Collects usage telemetry, performance metrics, and execution logs
"""

import json
import logging
import time
from datetime import datetime, timezone
from typing import Dict, Any, Optional, List
from dataclasses import asdict
import uuid
import asyncio
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor

from google.cloud import bigquery
from google.cloud import pubsub_v1
import redis

from ..data_lake.schema_definitions import (
    BronzeTelemetry,
    BronzeAgentPerformance,
    BronzeExecutionLog,
    TelemetryEventType,
    AgentType,
    ExecutionStatus
)


class TelemetryCollector:
    """Collects and ingests telemetry data into the data lake"""
    
    def __init__(self, config: Dict[str, Any]):
        self.config = config
        self.logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
        
        # Initialize clients
        self.bq_client = bigquery.Client()
        self.pubsub_publisher = pubsub_v1.PublisherClient()
        self.redis_client = redis.Redis(
            host=config['redis']['host'],
            port=config['redis']['port'],
            decode_responses=True
        )
        
        # Thread pool for async operations
        self.executor = ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=10)

# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Security by Design & Hardening

## 1. Threat Modeling da Arquitetura V11 (STRIDE)

### Documento de Threat Modeling

**Feature:** DIYAPP V11 Core - Sistema de Automação de Squads Autônomas
**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Responsável:** Especialista em Segurança Sênior

### 1.1 Diagrama de Arquitetura

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                            CLIENTE (Browser)                            │
│                    (React/Vue.js + Service Worker)                      │
└─────────────────┬─────────────────────────────────────────┬─────────────┘
                  │ HTTPS/TLS 1.3                           │ HTTPS/TLS 1.3
                  ▼                                         ▼
┌─────────────────────────────────┐         ┌─────────────────────────────┐
│        API GATEWAY (NGINX)      │         │     AUTH SERVICE (OIDC)     │
│  - Rate Limiting                │         │  - OAuth2.0 / OIDC Provider │
│  - WAF (ModSecurity)            │         │  - MFA (TOTP, WebAuthn)     │
│  - Request Validation           │         │  - Session Management       │
│  - CORS Policies                │         └──────────────┬──────────────┘
└──────────────┬──────────────────┘                        │
               │                                           │
               │ Service-to-Service                       │ JWT Validation
               │ mTLS                                     │
               ▼                                           ▼
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                          KUBERNETES CLUSTER                             │
│                                                                         │
│  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐  ┌──────────────┐  ┌─────────────┐  │
│  │   ORCHESTR   │  │   ANALYTICS  │  │    LLM API   │  │   TASK      │  │
│  │   SERVICE    │  │   SERVICE    │  │   SERVICE    │  │   QUEUE     │  │
│  │              │  │              │  │              │  │             │  │
│  └──────┬───────┘  └──────┬───────┘  └──────┬───────┘  └──────┬──────┘  │
│         │                  │                  │                  │       │
│  ┌──────▼───────┐  ┌──────▼───────┐  ┌──────▼───────┐  ┌──────▼──────┐  │
│  │   POSTGRES   │  │   REDIS      │  │   VAULT      │  │   RABBITMQ  │  │
│  │   (Primary)  │  │   (Cache)    │  │   (Secrets)  │  │             │  │
│  └──────────────┘  └──────────────┘  └──────────────┘  └─────────────┘  │
│         │                  │                  │                  │       │
│  ┌──────▼───────┐  ┌──────▼───────┐                            │       │
│  │   POSTGRES   │  │   REDIS      │                            │       │
│  │   (Replica)  │  │   Sentinel   │                            │       │
│  └──────────────┘  └──────────────┘                            │       │
│                                                                         │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

### 1.2 Análise STRIDE

#### **S - Spoofing (Personificação)**
- **Ameaça S1:** Ataque de credential stuffing na autenticação
- **Ameaça S2:** Token JWT roubado/reutilizado
- **Ameaça S3:** mTLS certificate spoofing entre serviços
- **Controles:**
  - MFA obrigatório para todas as contas
  - JWT com vida curta (15min) + refresh tokens rotativos
  - Certificados mTLS emitidos por CA interna com rotação automática
  - Rate limiting em endpoints de login (10 tentativas/hora/IP)

#### **T - Tampering (Manipulação)**
- **Ameaça T1:** Manipulação de dados em trânsito
- **Ameaça T2:** SQL/NoSQL injection
- **Ameaça T3:** Manipulação de prompts LLM (prompt injection)
- **Controles:**
  - TLS 1.3 em todas as comunicações
  - Prepared statements/ORM com parametrização
  - Validação de schema em todas as APIs (JSON Schema/OpenAPI)
  - Sanitização de inputs LLM com allowlist de caracteres

#### **R - Repudiation (Não Repúdio)**
- **Ameaça R1:** Usuário nega ação executada
- **Ameaça R2:** Admin nega modificação de configuração
- **Controles:**
  - Logs de auditoria imutáveis (WAL + SIEM)
  - Assinatura digital em logs críticos
  - Retenção de logs por 7 anos (compliance)

#### **I - Information Disclosure (Divulgação)**
- **Ameaça I1:** Vazamento de dados PII via API
- **Ameaça I2:** Logs contendo dados sensíveis
- **Ameaça I3:** LLM vazando dados do contexto
- **Controles:**
  - Criptografia AES-256-GCM para dados em repouso
  - Máscara de dados sensíveis em logs
  - Controle de acesso baseado em atributos (ABAC)
  - DLP scanning em outputs LLM

#### **D - Denial of Service (Negação de Serviço)**
- **Ameaça D1:** Ataque DDoS na API Gateway
- **Ameaça D2:** Resource exhaustion em serviços LLM
- **Ameaça D3:** Queue flooding no RabbitMQ
- **Controles:**
  - WAF com rate limiting adaptativo
  - Circuit breakers em todas as chamadas de serviço
  - Quotas por usuário/organização
  - Auto-scaling com limites máximos

#### **E - Elevation of Privilege (Elevação de Privilégio)**
- **Ameaça E1:** Bypass de autorização RBAC
- **Ameaça E2:** Container escape no Kubernetes
- **Ameaça E3:** LLM executando ações privilegiadas
- **Controles:**
  - Verificação de permissão em cada camada (defesa em profundidade)
  - Pod Security Policies no Kubernetes
  - LLM nunca tem acesso direto a operações críticas
  - Princípio do menor privilégio em todos os serviços

### 1.3 Riscos Aceitos Documentados

| ID  | Risco | Justificativa | Proprietário |
|-----|-------|---------------|--------------|
| RA1 | LLM pode gerar conteúdo não intencional com probabilidade baixa | Guardrails implementados reduzem probabilidade para <0.1% | Product Owner |
| RA2 | Dependências de terceiros podem conter vulnerabilidades não detectadas | Scanner Snyk + monitoramento contínuo mitigam | Security Team |

---

### 2.2 Código Principal de Segurança

#### **src/auth/oauth2.js** - Sistema de Autenticação OAuth2.0/OIDC
```javascript
const crypto = require('crypto');
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const { VaultClient } = require('../vault/integration');

class OAuth2Security {
  constructor() {
    this.vault = new VaultClient();
    this.jwtSecret = null;
    this.refreshTokens = new Map();
    this.failedAttempts = new Map();
  }

  async initialize() {
    // Carregar segredos do Vault
    this.jwtSecret = await this.vault.getSecret('jwt/signing-key');
    this.encryptionKey = await this.vault.getSecret('data/encryption-key');
    
    // Configurar políticas de senha
    this.passwordPolicy = {
      minLength: 12,
      requireUpper: true,
      requireLower: true,
      requireNumbers: true,
      requireSpecial: true,
      preventReuse: 5,
      maxAgeDays: 90
    };
  }

  async authenticate(username, password, ipAddress) {
    // Rate limiting por IP
    if (this.isRateLimited(ipAddress)) {
      throw new Error('Too many attempts. Please try again later.');
    }

    // Verificar credenciais com prevenção de timing attacks
    const user = await this.verifyCredentials(username, password);
    
    if (!user) {
      this.recordFailedAttempt(ipAddress);
      throw new Error('Invalid credentials');
    }

    // Verificar se MFA é necessário
    if (user.requiresMFA) {
      return { requiresMFA: true, mfaMethods: user.mfaMethods };
    }

    // Gerar tokens
    const tokens = await this.generateTokens(user);
    
    // Registrar login bem-sucedido
    await this.auditLog('LOGIN_SUCCESS', {
      userId: user.id,
      ip: ipAddress,
      userAgent: this.getUserAgent()
    });

    return tokens;
  }

  async generateTokens(user) {
    const accessToken = jwt.sign(
      {
        sub: user.id,
        email: user.email,
        roles: user.roles,
        permissions: user.permissions
      },
      this.jwtSecret,
      {
        algorithm: 'RS256',
        expiresIn: '15m', // Vida curta para access tokens
        issuer: 'diyapp-v11',
        audience: 'diyapp-api'
      }
    );

    // Refresh token rotativo
    const refreshToken = crypto.randomBytes(64).toString('hex');
    const refreshTokenHash = this.hashToken(refreshToken);
    
    // Armazenar hash no vault com TTL
    await this.vault.storeRefreshToken(refreshTokenHash, {
      userId: user.id,
      expiresAt: Date.now() + (7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000), // 7 dias
      family: crypto.randomBytes(16).toString('hex') // Família de tokens para detecção de reutilização
    });

    return {
      access_token: accessToken,
      refresh_token: refreshToken,
      token_type: 'Bearer',
      expires_in: 900
    };
  }

  async verifyMFA(userId, method, code) {
    const user = await this.getUser(userId);
    
    switch (method) {
      case 'TOTP':
        return this.verifyTOTP(user.mfaSecret, code);
      case 'WebAuthn':
        return this.verifyWebAuthn(user.webauthnCredentials, code);
      case 'SMS':
        return this.verifySMSCode(user.phone, code);
      default:
        throw new Error('Invalid MFA method');
    }
  }

  hashToken(token) {
    return crypto
      .createHash('sha512')
      .update(token + this.jwtSecret)
      .digest('hex');
  }

  isRateLimited(ipAddress) {
    const attempts = this.failedAttempts.get(ipAddress) || [];
    const recentAttempts = attempts.filter(t => 
      Date.now() - t < 3600000 // Última hora
    );
    
    return recentAttempts.length >= 10;
  }

  recordFailedAttempt(ipAddress) {
    const attempts = this.failedAttempts.get(ipAddress) || [];
    attempts.push(Date.now());
    this.failedAttempts.set(ipAddress, attempts);
    
    // Limpar tentativas antigas
    setTimeout(() => {
      const current = this.failedAttempts.get(ipAddress) || [];
      this.failedAttempts.set(
        ipAddress, 
        current.filter(t => Date.now() - t < 3600000)
      );
    }, 3600000);
  }

  async auditLog(action, metadata) {
    // Logs imutáveis com assinatura digital
    const logEntry = {
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      action,
      metadata,
      hash: this.createLogHash(action, metadata)
    };

    // Enviar para SIEM e armazenar localmente
    await Promise.all([
      this.sendToSIEM(logEntry),
      this.storeInWAL(logEntry)
    ]);
  }

  createLogHash(action, metadata) {
    const data = JSON.stringify({ action, metadata, timestamp: new Date().toISOString() });
    return crypto
      .createHmac('sha256', this.jwtSecret)
      .update(data)
      .digest('hex');
  }
}

module.exports = OAuth2Security;
```

#### **src/auth/mfa.js** - Implementação de MFA
```javascript
const speakeasy = require('speakeasy');
const qrcode = require('qrcode');
const { WebAuthn } = require('@simplewebauthn/server');

class MFASecurity {
  constructor() {
    this.webauthn = new WebAuthn({
      rpName: 'DIYAPP V11',
      rpID: process.env.RP_ID || 'localhost',
      origin: process.env.ORIGIN || 'https://diyapp.local'
    });
  }

  async setupTOTP(userId) {
    const secret = speakeasy.generateSecret({
      name: `DIYAPP:${userId}`,
      length: 32
    });

    // Gerar QR Code
    const qrCodeUrl = await qrcode.toDataURL(secret.otpauth_url);

    return {
      secret: secret.base32,
      qrCode: qrCodeUrl,
      backupCodes: this.generateBackupCodes()
    };
  }

  verifyTOTP(secret, token) {
    return speakeasy.totp.verify({
      secret,
      encoding: 'base32',
      token,
      window: 1 // Permitir 30 segundos de drift
    });
  }

  async setupWebAuthn(userId, username) {
    const options = await this.webauthn.registrationCeremony({
      userId,
      username,
      userDisplayName: username
    });

    return options;
  }

  async verifyWebAuthnResponse(response, expectedChallenge) {
    return await this.webauthn.verifyRegistration(response, expectedChallenge);
  }

  generateBackupCodes() {
    const codes = [];
    for (let i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
      codes.push(crypto.randomBytes(4).toString('hex').toUpperCase());
    }
    
    // Armazenar hash dos códigos
    const hashedCodes = codes.map(code => 
      crypto.createHash('sha256').update(code).digest('hex')
    );

    return { codes, hashedCodes };
  }

  async sendSMSCode(phoneNumber) {
    const code = Math.floor(100000 + Math.random() * 900000).toString();
    const ttl = 300; // 5 minutos
    
    // Armazenar no Redis com TTL
    await redis.setex(`mfa:sms:${phoneNumber}`, ttl, code);
    
    // Enviar SMS via Twilio ou similar
    await this.smsProvider.send({
      to: phoneNumber,
      body: `Your DIYAPP verification code is: ${code}. Valid for 5 minutes.`
    });

    return { method: 'SMS', ttl };
  }

  verifySMSCode(phoneNumber, code) {
    return redis.get(`mfa:sms:${phoneNumber}`).then(storedCode => {
      if (!storedCode) return false;
      return storedCode === code;
    });
  }
}

module.exports = MFASecurity;
```

#### **src/encryption/tls-config.js** - Configuração TLS 1.3
```javascript
const fs = require('fs');
const https = require('https');
const tls = require('tls');

class TLSSecurity {
  constructor() {
    this.ciphers = [
      'TLS_AES_256_GCM_SHA384',
      'TLS_CHACHA20_POLY1305_SHA256',
      'TLS_AES_128_GCM_SHA256'
    ].join(':');

    this.secureProtocol = 'TLSv1.3';
  }

  createSecureServer(app

│   └── environment/
├── scripts/
│   ├── ci/
│   ├── deployment/
│   └── monitoring/
├── docker/
│   ├── staging/
│   └── test-environments/
├── docs/
│   └── test-strategy/
└── index.html
```

## 1. Plano de Testes V11 - Documento de Estratégia

**docs/test-strategy/V11-TEST-STRATEGY.md**

```markdown
# DIYAPP V11 - Estratégia de Testes

## Visão Geral
Estratégia de testes para garantir estabilidade 100% autônoma da V11, seguindo a pirâmide de testes da squad.

## Pirâmide de Testes V11
- **Unitários (60%)**: Cobertura mínima 80% (90% lógica de negócio)
- **Integração (25%)**: APIs, banco, serviços externos
- **E2E (10%)**: Fluxos críticos do usuário
- **Exploratório (5%)**: Sessões guiadas por hipótese

## Fluxos Críticos para E2E
1. Autenticação e autorização
2. Criação de projeto DIY
3. Execução de agente autônomo
4. Integração com WhatsApp
5. Geração de código com LLM
6. Deploy automático
7. Monitoramento e alertas

## Ambiente de Staging
- Réplica exata da produção
- Dados anonimizados de produção
- Mesmo hardware/cloud specs
- Mesmas configurações de segurança

## Gates de Qualidade no Pipeline
1. PR: Unit + Integration tests (máx 10min)
2. Merge: E2E smoke tests (máx 15min)
3. Staging: Full regression (máx 30min)
4. Production: Smoke tests pós-deploy (máx 5min)

## Métricas de Qualidade
- Escape rate: ≤ 1 bug crítico/alto por sprint
- Tempo CI: < 10 minutos
- Testes flaky: 0 em aberto
- Cobertura LLM: 100% features com golden dataset
```

## 2. Configuração do Ambiente de Staging

**docker/staging/docker-compose.staging.yml**

```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  # Banco de dados
  postgres-staging:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: diyapp_staging
      POSTGRES_USER: diyapp
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${DB_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - postgres-data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
      - ./init-scripts:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d
    ports:
      - "5433:5432"
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U diyapp"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  # Redis para cache e filas
  redis-staging:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    ports:
      - "6380:6379"
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "ping"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  # Aplicação principal
  app-staging:
    build:
      context: ../..
      dockerfile: docker/staging/Dockerfile.staging
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: staging
      DATABASE_URL: postgresql://diyapp:${DB_PASSWORD}@postgres-staging:5432/diyapp_staging
      REDIS_URL: redis://redis-staging:6379
      API_PORT: 3001
    ports:
      - "3001:3001"
    depends_on:
      postgres-staging:
        condition: service_healthy
      redis-staging:
        condition: service_healthy
    volumes:
      - ../../logs:/app/logs
      - ../../uploads:/app/uploads

  # Mock de serviços externos
  mock-services:
    image: mockserver/mockserver:latest
    ports:
      - "1080:1080"
    command: -serverPort 1080 -logLevel INFO
    volumes:
      - ./mock-config:/config

  # Monitoramento
  prometheus-staging:
    image: prom/prometheus:latest
    ports:
      - "9091:9090"
    volumes:
      - ./prometheus.yml:/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml

  grafana-staging:
    image: grafana/grafana:latest
    ports:
      - "3002:3000"
    environment:
      GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD: ${GRAFANA_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - grafana-data:/var/lib/grafana

volumes:
  postgres-data:
  grafana-data:
```

## 3. Configuração de Testes Unitários e Integração

**config/jest.config.js**

```javascript
module.exports = {
  preset: 'ts-jest',
  testEnvironment: 'node',
  collectCoverage: true,
  coverageThreshold: {
    global: {
      branches: 80,
      functions: 80,
      lines: 80,
      statements: 80
    },
    './src/business-logic/': {
      branches: 90,
      functions: 90,
      lines: 90,
      statements: 90
    }
  },
  coverageDirectory: 'coverage',
  coverageReporters: ['text', 'lcov', 'html'],
  testMatch: [
    '**/__tests__/**/*.test.[jt]s?(x)',
    '**/?(*.)+(spec|test).[jt]s?(x)'
  ],
  setupFilesAfterEnv: ['./src/tests/setup/jest.setup.js'],
  globalSetup: './src/tests/setup/jest.global-setup.js',
  globalTeardown: './src/tests/setup/jest.global-teardown.js',
  testTimeout: 10000,
  maxWorkers: '50%',
  verbose: true,
  reporters: [
    'default',
    ['jest-junit', {
      outputDirectory: 'test-results/jest',
      outputName: 'jest-results.xml'
    }]
  ]
};
```

**src/tests/unit/business-logic/agent-orchestrator.test.js**

```javascript
const { AgentOrchestrator } = require('../../../business-logic/agent-orchestrator');
const { TaskValidator } = require('../../../business-logic/validators');

describe('AgentOrchestrator - Unit Tests', () => {
  let orchestrator;
  let mockLLMService;
  let mockCodeGenerator;

  beforeEach(() => {
    mockLLMService = {
      generateInstruction: jest.fn(),
      validateOutput: jest.fn()
    };

    mockCodeGenerator = {
      generateCode: jest.fn(),
      validateSyntax: jest.fn()
    };

    orchestrator = new AgentOrchestrator({
      llmService: mockLLMService,
      codeGenerator: mockCodeGenerator
    });
  });

  describe('Task Validation', () => {
    test('should accept valid DIY task', async () => {
      const validTask = {
        type: 'web-app',
        requirements: 'Create a todo app with React',
        complexity: 'medium',
        deadline: new Date(Date.now() + 86400000)
      };

      const result = await orchestrator.validateTask(validTask);
      expect(result.isValid).toBe(true);
      expect(result.errors).toHaveLength(0);
    });

    test('should reject task without requirements', async () => {
      const invalidTask = {
        type: 'web-app',
        complexity: 'medium'
      };

      const result = await orchestrator.validateTask(invalidTask);
      expect(result.isValid).toBe(false);
      expect(result.errors).toContain('Requirements are required');
    });

    test('should reject task with past deadline', async () => {
      const invalidTask = {
        type: 'web-app',
        requirements: 'Create app',
        deadline: new Date(Date.now() - 86400000)
      };

      const result = await orchestrator.validateTask(invalidTask);
      expect(result.isValid).toBe(false);
      expect(result.errors).toContain('Deadline must be in the future');
    });
  });

  describe('Agent Assignment', () => {
    test('should assign correct agent based on task type', async () => {
      const webTask = { type: 'web-app', requirements: 'React app' };
      const mobileTask = { type: 'mobile-app', requirements: 'React Native app' };
      const dataTask = { type: 'data-pipeline', requirements: 'ETL process' };

      const webAgent = await orchestrator.assignAgent(webTask);
      const mobileAgent = await orchestrator.assignAgent(mobileTask);
      const dataAgent = await orchestrator.assignAgent(dataTask);

      expect(webAgent.specialization).toBe('frontend');
      expect(mobileAgent.specialization).toBe('mobile');
      expect(dataAgent.specialization).toBe('data-engineering');
    });

    test('should handle concurrent agent assignments', async () => {
      const tasks = Array(10).fill(null).map((_, i) => ({
        type: 'web-app',
        requirements: `Task ${i}`,
        complexity: 'simple'
      }));

      const assignments = await Promise.all(
        tasks.map(task => orchestrator.assignAgent(task))
      );

      expect(assignments).toHaveLength(10);
      expect(new Set(assignments.map(a => a.id)).size).toBeGreaterThan(1);
    });
  });

  describe('LLM Integration', () => {
    test('should generate valid instructions from requirements', async () => {
      const requirements = 'Create a REST API with Node.js and PostgreSQL';
      
      mockLLMService.generateInstruction.mockResolvedValue({
        steps: [
          'Setup Node.js project',
          'Install Express and pg',
          'Create database schema',
          'Implement CRUD endpoints',
          'Add error handling'
        ],
        technologies: ['Node.js', 'Express', 'PostgreSQL', 'Jest'],
        estimatedHours: 8
      });

      const instructions = await orchestrator.generateInstructions(requirements);
      
      expect(instructions).toHaveProperty('steps');
      expect(instructions.steps).toHaveLength(5);
      expect(instructions.technologies).toContain('Node.js');
      expect(instructions.estimatedHours).toBeGreaterThan(0);
    });

    test('should handle LLM timeout gracefully', async () => {
      mockLLMService.generateInstruction.mockImplementation(() => 
        new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 31000))
      );

      await expect(
        orchestrator.generateInstructions('test', { timeout: 30000 })
      ).rejects.toThrow('LLM timeout');
    });
  });
});
```

## 4. Testes de Integração

**src/tests/integration/api/projects-api.test.js**

```javascript
const request = require('supertest');
const { createTestApp } = require('../../setup/integration-setup');
const { createTestUser, generateAuthToken } = require('../../helpers/auth-helper');
const { createTestProject } = require('../../helpers/project-helper');

describe('Projects API - Integration Tests', () => {
  let app;
  let testUser;
  let authToken;
  let db;

  beforeAll(async () => {
    ({ app, db } = await createTestApp());
    testUser = await createTestUser(db);
    authToken = generateAuthToken(testUser);
  });

  afterAll(async () => {
    await db.close();
  });

  beforeEach(async () => {
    await db.reset();
  });

  describe('POST /api/v1/projects', () => {
    test('should create new project with valid data', async () => {
      const projectData = {
        name: 'Test DIY Project',
        description: 'A test project for integration testing',
        type: 'web-app',
        requirements: 'Create a React app with TypeScript',
        deadline: new Date(Date.now() + 86400000).toISOString()
      };

      const response = await request(app)
        .post('/api/v1/projects')
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${authToken}`)
        .send(projectData)
        .expect(201);

      expect(response.body).toHaveProperty('id');
      expect(response.body.name).toBe(projectData.name);
      expect(response.body.status).toBe('pending');
      expect(response.body.createdBy).toBe(testUser.id);
    });

    test('should reject project without authentication', async () => {
      const response = await request(app)
        .post('/api/v1/projects')
        .send({ name: 'Test' })
        .expect(401);

      expect(response.body.error).toBe('Authentication required');
    });

    test('should validate project requirements', async () => {
      const invalidData = {
        name: 'Test',
        type: 'invalid-type'
      };

      const response = await request(app)
        .post('/api/v1/projects')
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${authToken}`)
        .send(invalidData)
        .expect(400);

      expect(response.body.errors).toContain('Invalid project type');
    });
  });

  describe('GET /api/v1/projects/:id', () => {
    test('should retrieve project by ID', async () => {
      const project = await createTestProject(db, testUser.id);

      const response = await request(app)
        .get(`/api/v1/projects/${project.id}`)
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${authToken}`)
        .expect(200);

      expect(response.body.id).toBe(project.id);
      expect(response.body.name).toBe(project.name);
    });

    test('should return 404 for non-existent project', async () => {
      const response = await request(app)
        .get('/api/v1/projects/999999')
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${authToken}`)
        .expect(404);

      expect(response.body.error).toBe('Project not found');
    });

    test('should enforce project ownership', async () => {
      const otherUser = await createTestUser(db, { email: 'other@test.com' });
      const project = await createTestProject(db, otherUser.id);

      const response = await request(app)
        .get(`/api/v1/projects/${project.id}`)
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${authToken}`)
        .expect(403);

      expect(response.body.error).toBe('Access denied');
    });
  });

  describe('WebSocket - Real-time Updates', () => {
    test('should receive project status updates', (done) => {
      const WebSocket = require('ws');
      const ws = new WebSocket(`ws://localhost:${process.env.PORT}/ws/projects`);

      ws.on('open', () => {
        ws.send(JSON.stringify({
          type: 'auth',
          token: authToken
        }));
      });

      ws.on('message', (data) => {
        const message = JSON.parse(data);
        if (message.type === 'project.update') {
          expect(message.data).toHaveProperty('projectId');
          expect(message.data).toHaveProperty('status');
          ws.close();
          done();
        }
      });

      // Simulate project update
      setTimeout(() => {
        // This would be triggered by the application
      }, 100);
    });
  });
});
```

## 5. Testes E2E com Playwright

**src/tests/e2e/playwright/auth.spec.js**

```javascript
const { test, expect } = require('@playwright/test');
const { STAGING_URL } = require('../../config/environment');

test.describe('Authentication E2E Flow', () => {
  test.beforeEach(async ({ page }) => {
    await page.goto(`${STAGING_URL}/login`);
  });

  test('should login successfully with valid credentials', async ({ page }) => {
    // Arrange
    await page.fill('#email', 'test@example.com');
    await page.fill('#password', 'TestPass123!');

    // Act
    await page.click('button[type="submit"]');

    // Assert
    await expect(page).toHaveURL(`${STAGING_URL}/dashboard`);
    await expect(page.locator('.user-profile')).toBeVisible();
    
    // Verify session cookie
    const cookies = await page.context().cookies();
    const sessionCookie = cookies.find(c => c.name === 'session_id');
    expect(sessionCookie).toBeTruthy();
    expect(sessionCookie.httpOnly).toBe(true);
    expect(sessionCookie.secure).toBe(true);
  });

  test('should show error with invalid credentials', async ({ page }) => {
    await page.fill('#email', 'wrong@example.com');
    await page.fill('#password', 'WrongPass');
    await page.click('button[type="submit"]');

    await expect(page.locator('.error-message')).toBeVisible();
    await expect(page.locator('.error-message')).toContainText('Invalid credentials');
    await expect(page).toHaveURL(`${STAGING_URL}/login`);
  });

  test('should enforce password complexity', async ({ page }) => {
    await page.fill('#email', 'test@example.com');
    await page.fill('#password', 'simple');
    await page.click('button[

                            <small class="text-muted">Documentação sempre atual</small>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
            
            <!-- Recent Updates -->
            <div class="card mb-4">
                <div class="card-header bg-primary text-white">
                    <i class="fas fa-history me-2"></i>Atualizações Recentes
                </div>

        <!-- API Documentation -->

    <!-- JavaScript -->
    <script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/bootstrap@5.1.3/dist/js/bootstrap.bundle.min.js"></script>
    <script>
        // Atualizar timestamp
        document.getElementById('last-update').textContent = new Date().toLocaleString('pt-BR');
        document.getElementById('sync-time').textContent = new Date().toLocaleTimeString('pt-BR');
        
        // Simular dados de atualizações recentes
        const recentUpdates = [
            { date: '2024-01-15 14:30', component: 'API /agents', change: 'Adicionado suporte a WebSocket', status: 'Ativo' },
            { date: '2024-01-15 11:15', component: 'Guia de Deployment', change: 'Atualizado para Kubernetes 1.28', status: 'Revisado' },
            { date: '2024-01-14 16:45', component: 'Runbook #3', change: 'Procedimento de rollback otimizado', status: 'Publicado' },
            { date: '2024-01-14 09:20', component: 'OpenAPI Spec', change: 'Documentados 5 novos endpoints', status: 'Sincronizado' }
        ];
        
        const tbody = document.getElementById('recent-updates');
        recentUpdates.forEach(update => {
            const row = document.createElement('tr');
            row.innerHTML = `
                <td>${update.date}</td>
                <td><strong>${update.component}</strong></td>
                <td>${update.change}</td>
                <td><span class="badge bg-success">${update.status}</span></td>
            `;
            tbody.appendChild(row);
        });
        
        // Botão de sincronização
        document.getElementById('sync-docs').addEventListener('click', function() {
            const btn = this;
            const originalText = btn.innerHTML;
            
            btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-spinner fa-spin me-1"></i> Sincronizando...';
            btn.disabled = true;
            
            // Simular requisição de sincronização
            setTimeout(() => {
                btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-check me-1"></i> Sincronizado!';
                btn.className = 'btn btn-success btn-sm w-100 mb-2';
                
                // Atualizar timestamp
                const now = new Date();
                document.getElementById('last-update').textContent = now.toLocaleString('pt-BR');
                document.getElementById('sync-time').textContent = now.toLocaleTimeString('pt-BR');
                
                // Restaurar após 3 segundos
                setTimeout(() => {
                    btn.innerHTML = originalText;
                    btn.className = 'btn btn-warning btn-sm w-100 mb-2';
                    btn.disabled = false;
                }, 3000);
            }, 1500);
        });
        
        // Testar endpoints
        document.querySelectorAll('.try-endpoint').forEach(btn => {
            btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
                const endpoint = this.getAttribute('data-endpoint');
                const method = this.getAttribute('data-method');

            // Implementação de busca seria conectada ao backend
            console.log('Buscando por:', searchTerm);
        });

## 1. Sistema de Retenção de Dados Automatizado (LGPD/GDPR Compliant)

### `src/compliance/data_retention.py`

```python
"""
Sistema de Retenção de Dados Automatizado - Conformidade LGPD/GDPR
Implementa políticas de retenção baseadas em finalidade e exclusão automática
"""

import asyncio
import logging
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from enum import Enum
from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Any
from dataclasses import dataclass
import json

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class DataCategory(Enum):
    """Categorias de dados pessoais conforme LGPD"""
    IDENTIFICACAO = "identificacao"
    CONTATO = "contato"
    FINANCEIRO = "financeiro"
    COMPORTAMENTO = "comportamento"
    SENSIVEL = "sensivel"  # Dados sensíveis - tratamento especial
    ANONIMO = "anonimo"    # Dados anonimizados

class RetentionPolicy(Enum):
    """Políticas de retenção baseadas em finalidade"""
    # Base Legal: Contrato (Art. 7º, V LGPD)
    CONTRATO_ATIVO = timedelta(days=365*5)  # 5 anos após término
    # Base Legal: Obrigação Legal (Art. 7º, II LGPD)
    FISCAL = timedelta(days=365*10)         # 10 anos
    # Base Legal: Legítimo Interesse (Art. 7º, IX LGPD)
    ANALYTICS = timedelta(days=730)         # 2 anos
    # Base Legal: Consentimento (Art. 7º, I LGPD)
    MARKETING = timedelta(days=180)         # 6 meses após revogação
    # Dados de sessão
    SESSION = timedelta(days=30)            # 30 dias
    # Logs de auditoria
    AUDIT_LOG = timedelta(days=180)         # 6 meses (mínimo LGPD)

@dataclass
class DataSubject:
    """Titular de dados"""
    id: str
    email: str
    created_at: datetime
    consent_given: bool
    consent_date: Optional[datetime]
    data_categories: List[DataCategory]

@dataclass
class RetentionRecord:
    """Registro de retenção para auditoria"""
    data_id: str
    subject_id: str
    category: DataCategory
    collected_at: datetime
    purpose: str
    legal_basis: str
    policy: RetentionPolicy
    expires_at: datetime
    deleted: bool = False
    deleted_at: Optional[datetime] = None

class DataRetentionManager:
    """Gerenciador central de retenção e exclusão de dados"""
    
    def __init__(self, db_connection):
        self.db = db_connection
        self.retention_queue = asyncio.Queue()
        self.active = True
        
    async def initialize(self):
        """Inicializa o sistema de retenção"""
        logger.info("Inicializando Data Retention Manager")
        # Cria tabelas necessárias
        await self._create_tables()
        # Inicia worker de limpeza
        asyncio.create_task(self._retention_worker())
        
    async def _create_tables(self):
        """Cria tabelas de compliance no banco de dados"""
        create_tables_sql = """
        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS retention_records (
            id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
            data_id TEXT NOT NULL,
            subject_id TEXT NOT NULL,
            category TEXT NOT NULL,
            collected_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
            purpose TEXT NOT NULL,
            legal_basis TEXT NOT NULL,
            policy TEXT NOT NULL,
            expires_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
            deleted BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
            deleted_at TIMESTAMP,
            created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
        );
        
        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS data_subjects (
            id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
            email TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL,
            created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
            consent_given BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
            consent_date TIMESTAMP,
            data_categories JSON,
            updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
        );
        
        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS consent_logs (
            id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
            subject_id TEXT NOT NULL,
            action TEXT NOT NULL,  -- 'granted', 'revoked', 'updated'
            scope JSON NOT NULL,   -- Escopos de consentimento
            ip_address TEXT,
            user_agent TEXT,
            timestamp TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
            FOREIGN KEY (subject_id) REFERENCES data_subjects(id)
        );
        
        CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_retention_expires ON retention_records(expires_at, deleted);
        CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_subject_consent ON data_subjects(consent_given, consent_date);
        """
        await self.db.executescript(create_tables_sql)
    
    async def register_data_collection(
        self,
        data_id: str,
        subject_id: str,
        category: DataCategory,
        purpose: str,
        legal_basis: str,
        policy: RetentionPolicy
    ) -> str:
        """
        Registra nova coleta de dados no sistema de retenção
        
        Args:
            data_id: Identificador único do dado
            subject_id: ID do titular
            category: Categoria do dado
            purpose: Finalidade do tratamento
            legal_basis: Base legal (LGPD Art. 7)
            policy: Política de retenção aplicável
            
        Returns:
            ID do registro de retenção
        """
        from uuid import uuid4
        
        record_id = str(uuid4())
        collected_at = datetime.utcnow()
        expires_at = collected_at + policy.value
        
        record = RetentionRecord(
            data_id=data_id,
            subject_id=subject_id,
            category=category,
            collected_at=collected_at,
            purpose=purpose,
            legal_basis=legal_basis,
            policy=policy,
            expires_at=expires_at
        )
        
        # Insere no banco de dados
        await self.db.execute(
            """
            INSERT INTO retention_records 
            (id, data_id, subject_id, category, collected_at, purpose, 
             legal_basis, policy, expires_at)
            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
            """,
            (
                record_id, record.data_id, record.subject_id, 
                record.category.value, record.collected_at.isoformat(),
                record.purpose, record.legal_basis, record.policy.name,
                record.expires_at.isoformat()
            )
        )
        
        logger.info(f"Registro de retenção criado: {record_id} para dado {data_id}")
        return record_id
    
    async def _retention_worker(self):
        """Worker que processa exclusões automáticas baseadas em políticas"""
        while self.active:
            try:
                # Verifica dados expirados a cada hora
                await asyncio.sleep(3600)
                
                expired_data = await self.db.execute_fetchall(
                    """
                    SELECT id, data_id, subject_id, category 
                    FROM retention_records 
                    WHERE expires_at <= ? AND deleted = FALSE
                    LIMIT 100
                    """,
                    (datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),)
                )
                
                for record in expired_data:
                    await self._delete_data(
                        record['id'],
                        record['data_id'],
                        record['subject_id'],
                        DataCategory(record['category']),
                        "retention_policy_expired"
                    )
                    
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"Erro no worker de retenção: {e}")
    
    async def _delete_data(
        self, 
        record_id: str, 
        data_id: str, 
        subject_id: str,
        category: DataCategory,
        reason: str
    ):
        """
        Executa exclusão segura de dados
        
        Args:
            record_id: ID do registro de retenção
            data_id: ID do dado a ser excluído
            subject_id: ID do titular
            category: Categoria do dado
            reason: Motivo da exclusão
        """
        try:
            # 1. Registra início da exclusão no log de auditoria
            await self._log_deletion_attempt(record_id, reason)
            
            # 2. Executa exclusão baseada na categoria
            if category == DataCategory.SENSIVEL:
                # Dados sensíveis: exclusão física + sobrescrita
                await self._secure_delete(data_id)
            else:
                # Dados regulares: exclusão lógica
                await self._logical_delete(data_id)
            
            # 3. Atualiza registro de retenção
            deleted_at = datetime.utcnow()
            await self.db.execute(
                """
                UPDATE retention_records 
                SET deleted = TRUE, deleted_at = ?
                WHERE id = ?
                """,
                (deleted_at.isoformat(), record_id)
            )
            
            # 4. Log de auditoria
            await self._log_audit_event(
                subject_id=subject_id,
                action="data_deletion",
                resource_type="personal_data",
                resource_id=data_id,
                details={
                    "reason": reason,
                    "category": category.value,
                    "method": "secure" if category == DataCategory.SENSIVEL else "logical"
                }
            )
            
            logger.info(f"Dado {data_id} excluído por motivo: {reason}")
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Falha na exclusão do dado {data_id}: {e}")
            await self._log_audit_event(
                subject_id=subject_id,
                action="deletion_failed",
                resource_type="personal_data",
                resource_id=data_id,
                details={"error": str(e), "reason": reason}
            )
    
    async def handle_subject_request(
        self,
        subject_id: str,
        request_type: str,  # 'access', 'deletion', 'correction', 'portability'
        data: Optional[Dict] = None
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """
        Processa solicitação de titular conforme LGPD Art. 18
        
        Args:
            subject_id: ID do titular
            request_type: Tipo de solicitação
            data: Dados adicionais para correção
            
        Returns:
            Resultado do processamento
        """
        from uuid import uuid4
        
        request_id = str(uuid4())
        start_time = datetime.utcnow()
        
        try:
            # Valida existência do titular
            subject = await self.db.execute_fetchone(
                "SELECT * FROM data_subjects WHERE id = ?",
                (subject_id,)
            )
            
            if not subject:
                return {
                    "success": False,
                    "error": "subject_not_found",
                    "request_id": request_id
                }
            
            # Processa conforme tipo de solicitação
            if request_type == "access":
                result = await self._process_access_request(subject_id)
            elif request_type == "deletion":
                result = await self._process_deletion_request(subject_id)
            elif request_type == "correction" and data:
                result = await self._process_correction_request(subject_id, data)
            elif request_type == "portability":
                result = await self._process_portability_request(subject_id)
            else:
                return {
                    "success": False,
                    "error": "invalid_request_type",
                    "request_id": request_id
                }
            
            # Registra a solicitação
            await self._log_subject_request(
                request_id=request_id,
                subject_id=subject_id,
                request_type=request_type,
                status="completed" if result["success"] else "failed",
                processing_time=(datetime.utcnow() - start_time).total_seconds()
            )
            
            result["request_id"] = request_id
            return result
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Erro processando solicitação {request_type}: {e}")
            return {
                "success": False,
                "error": str(e),
                "request_id": request_id
            }
    
    async def _process_access_request(self, subject_id: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Processa solicitação de acesso (LGPD Art. 18, I)"""
        # Coleta todos os dados do titular
        records = await self.db.execute_fetchall(
            """
            SELECT r.*, s.email as subject_email
            FROM retention_records r
            JOIN data_subjects s ON r.subject_id = s.id
            WHERE r.subject_id = ? AND r.deleted = FALSE
            ORDER BY r.collected_at DESC
            """,
            (subject_id,)
        )
        
        # Formata resposta conforme LGPD
        response = {
            "success": True,
            "data": [],
            "summary": {
                "total_records": len(records),
                "categories": {},
                "purposes": {}
            }
        }
        
        for record in records:
            data_entry = {
                "data_id": record['data_id'],
                "category": record['category'],
                "collected_at": record['collected_at'],
                "purpose": record['purpose'],
                "legal_basis": record['legal_basis'],
                "expires_at": record['expires_at'],
                "policy": record['policy']
            }
            response["data"].append(data_entry)
            
            # Atualiza sumários
            response["summary"]["categories"][record['category']] = \
                response["summary"]["categories"].get(record['category'], 0) + 1
            response["summary"]["purposes"][record['purpose']] = \
                response["summary"]["purposes"].get(record['purpose'], 0) + 1
        
        return response
    
    async def _log_audit_event(
        self,
        subject_id: str,
        action: str,
        resource_type: str,
        resource_id: str,
        details: Dict
    ):
        """Registra evento de auditoria"""
        from uuid import uuid4
        
        await self.db.execute(
            """
            INSERT INTO audit_logs 
            (id, subject_id, action, resource_type, resource_id, details, timestamp)
            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
            """,
            (
                str(uuid4()), subject_id, action, resource_type, 
                resource_id, json.dumps(details), datetime.utcnow().isoformat()
            )
        )
    
    async def generate_retention_report(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Gera relatório de conformidade de retenção"""
        # Estatísticas gerais
        stats = await self.db.execute_fetchone(
            """
            SELECT 
                COUNT(*) as total_records,
                SUM(CASE WHEN deleted THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as deleted_records,
                SUM(CASE WHEN expires_at <= ? THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as expired_records
            FROM retention_records
            """,
            (datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),)
        )
        
        # Distribuição por política
        policies = await self.db.execute_fetchall(
            """
            SELECT policy, COUNT(*) as count
            FROM retention_records
            WHERE deleted = FALSE
            GROUP BY policy
            """
        )
        
        # Próximas exclusões (7 dias)
        upcoming = await self.db.execute_fetchall(
            """
            SELECT data_id, subject_id, category, expires_at
            FROM retention_records
            WHERE deleted = FALSE 
            AND expires_at BETWEEN ? AND ?
            ORDER BY expires_at
            LIMIT 50
            """,
            (
                datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
                (datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(days=7)).isoformat()
            )
        )
        
        return {
            "generated_at": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
            "statistics": dict(stats) if stats else {},
            "policies": {p['policy']: p['count'] for p in policies},
            "upcoming_deletions": upcoming,
            "compliance_status": self._calculate_compliance_score(stats)
        }
    
    def _calculate_compliance_score(self, stats: Dict) -> str:
        """Calcula score de conformidade baseado em métricas"""
        if not stats:
            return "UNKNOWN"
        
        total = stats['total_records'] or 1
        deleted = stats['deleted_records'] or 0
        expired = stats['expired_records'] or 0
        
        # Métrica: % de dados expirados não excluídos
        expired_not_deleted = max(0, expired - deleted)
        non_compliance_ratio = expired_not_deleted / total
        
        if non_compliance_ratio == 0:
            return "COMPLIANT"
        elif non_compliance_ratio < 0.01:  # < 1%
            return "LOW_RISK"
        elif non_compliance_ratio < 0.05:  # < 5%
            return

### [Sessão Paralela: Compliance]
```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="pt-BR">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>DIYAPP V11 - Painel de Governança & Privacidade</title>
    <style>
        :root {
            --primary-color: #1a365d;
            --secondary-color: #2d3748;
            --accent-color: #3182ce;
            --danger-color: #e53e3e;
            --success-color: #38a169;
            --warning-color: #d69e2e;
            --bg-color: #f7fafc;
            --card-color: #ffffff;
            --border-color: #e2e8f0;
        }
        
        * {
            margin: 0;
            padding: 0;
            box-sizing: border-box;
            font-family: 'Segoe UI', system-ui, -apple-system, sans-serif;
        }
        
        body {
            background-color: var(--bg-color);
            color: var(--secondary-color);
            line-height: 1.6;
        }
        
        .container {
            max-width: 1200px;
            margin: 0 auto;
            padding: 20px;
        }
        
        header {
            background: linear-gradient(135deg, var(--primary-color), var(--secondary-color));
            color: white;
            padding: 2rem 0;

## 1. Política de Retenção de Dados (LGPD/GDPR Compliant)

### `src/compliance/data_retention.py`

```python
"""
Sistema de Retenção de Dados Automatizado - Conformidade LGPD/GDPR
"""
import asyncio
import logging
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Any
from enum import Enum
from dataclasses import dataclass
from sqlalchemy import create_engine, Column, String, DateTime, JSON, Boolean, Integer
from sqlalchemy.ext.declarative import declarative_base
from sqlalchemy.orm import sessionmaker
import json
import hashlib

# Configuração de logging
logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

Base = declarative_base()

class DataCategory(Enum):
    """Categorias de dados pessoais conforme LGPD"""
    IDENTIFICACAO = "identificacao"
    CONTATO = "contato"
    FINANCEIRO = "financeiro"
    COMPORTAMENTO = "comportamento"
    SENSIVEL = "sensivel"  # Dados sensíveis - Art. 5º, II LGPD
    INFANTIL = "infantil"  # Dados de crianças - Art. 14 LGPD

class RetentionPurpose(Enum):
    """Finalidades de processamento com base legal"""
    CONTRATO = "contrato"
    CONSENTIMENTO = "consentimento"
    LEGITIMO_INTERESSE = "legitimo_interesse"
    OBRIGACAO_LEGAL = "obrigacao_legal"

@dataclass
class RetentionPolicy:
    """Política de retenção específica por categoria de dados"""
    data_category: DataCategory
    purpose: RetentionPurpose
    retention_period_days: int
    auto_delete: bool
    legal_basis: str
    description: str
    requires_consent: bool

class DataRetentionPolicyModel(Base):
    """Modelo de política de retenção no banco de dados"""
    __tablename__ = 'data_retention_policies'
    
    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
    data_category = Column(String(50), nullable=False)
    purpose = Column(String(50), nullable=False)
    retention_period_days = Column(Integer, nullable=False)
    auto_delete = Column(Boolean, default=True)
    legal_basis = Column(String(200), nullable=False)
    description = Column(String(500))
    requires_consent = Column(Boolean, default=False)
    created_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
    updated_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow, onupdate=datetime.utcnow)

class DataRetentionManager:
    """Gerenciador central de políticas de retenção"""
    
    # Políticas padrão conforme LGPD
    DEFAULT_POLICIES = [
        RetentionPolicy(
            data_category=DataCategory.IDENTIFICACAO,
            purpose=RetentionPurpose.CONTRATO,
            retention_period_days=365 * 5,  # 5 anos após término do contrato
            auto_delete=True,
            legal_basis="Art. 7º, V LGPD - Execução de contrato",
            description="Dados de identificação para prestação de serviços",
            requires_consent=False
        ),
        RetentionPolicy(
            data_category=DataCategory.CONTATO,
            purpose=RetentionPurpose.CONSENTIMENTO,
            retention_period_days=365 * 2,  # 2 anos após último contato
            auto_delete=True,
            legal_basis="Art. 7º, I LGPD - Consentimento",
            description="Dados de contato para comunicação",
            requires_consent=True
        ),
        RetentionPolicy(
            data_category=DataCategory.FINANCEIRO,
            purpose=RetentionPurpose.OBRIGACAO_LEGAL,
            retention_period_days=365 * 10,  # 10 anos para fins fiscais
            auto_delete=False,  # Não deletar automaticamente - requer revisão
            legal_basis="Art. 7º, II LGPD - Obrigação legal",
            description="Dados financeiros para compliance fiscal",
            requires_consent=False
        ),
        RetentionPolicy(
            data_category=DataCategory.SENSIVEL,
            purpose=RetentionPurpose.CONSENTIMENTO,
            retention_period_days=365 * 1,  # 1 ano máximo para dados sensíveis
            auto_delete=True,
            legal_basis="Art. 11 LGPD - Consentimento específico",
            description="Dados sensíveis com consentimento explícito",
            requires_consent=True
        ),
        RetentionPolicy(
            data_category=DataCategory.INFANTIL,
            purpose=RetentionPurpose.CONSENTIMENTO,
            retention_period_days=365 * 1,  # 1 ano para dados infantis
            auto_delete=True,
            legal_basis="Art. 14 LGPD - Consentimento dos responsáveis",
            description="Dados de crianças com consentimento dos pais",
            requires_consent=True
        )
    ]
    
    def __init__(self, database_url: str):
        self.engine = create_engine(database_url)
        Base.metadata.create_all(self.engine)
        self.Session = sessionmaker(bind=self.engine)
        self._initialize_default_policies()
    
    def _initialize_default_policies(self):
        """Inicializa políticas padrão no banco de dados"""
        session = self.Session()
        try:
            for policy in self.DEFAULT_POLICIES:
                existing = session.query(DataRetentionPolicyModel).filter_by(
                    data_category=policy.data_category.value,
                    purpose=policy.purpose.value
                ).first()
                
                if not existing:
                    db_policy = DataRetentionPolicyModel(
                        data_category=policy.data_category.value,
                        purpose=policy.purpose.value,
                        retention_period_days=policy.retention_period_days,
                        auto_delete=policy.auto_delete,
                        legal_basis=policy.legal_basis,
                        description=policy.description,
                        requires_consent=policy.requires_consent
                    )
                    session.add(db_policy)
            
            session.commit()
            logger.info("Políticas de retenção inicializadas com sucesso")
        except Exception as e:
            session.rollback()
            logger.error(f"Erro ao inicializar políticas: {e}")
        finally:
            session.close()
    
    async def apply_retention_policy(self, user_id: str, data_category: str, 
                                   collected_at: datetime) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """
        Aplica política de retenção e calcula data de expiração
        """
        session = self.Session()
        try:
            policy = session.query(DataRetentionPolicyModel).filter_by(
                data_category=data_category
            ).first()
            
            if not policy:
                raise ValueError(f"Política não encontrada para categoria: {data_category}")
            
            expiration_date = collected_at + timedelta(days=policy.retention_period_days)
            
            retention_record = {
                "user_id": user_id,
                "data_category": data_category,
                "collected_at": collected_at.isoformat(),
                "expires_at": expiration_date.isoformat(),
                "policy_id": policy.id,
                "auto_delete": policy.auto_delete,
                "legal_basis": policy.legal_basis,
                "requires_review": not policy.auto_delete
            }
            
            logger.info(f"Política aplicada para usuário {user_id}: {retention_record}")
            return retention_record
            
        finally:
            session.close()
    
    async def find_expired_data(self) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """
        Encontra dados que expiraram e precisam ser tratados
        """
        # Esta função seria integrada com o sistema de banco de dados real
        # Simulação de busca por dados expirados
        expired_data = []
        
        # Lógica real implementaria query no banco
        # SELECT * FROM user_data WHERE expires_at < NOW()
        
        return expired_data
    
    async def execute_data_deletion(self, user_id: str, data_category: str) -> bool:
        """
        Executa exclusão segura de dados conforme política
        """
        try:
            # 1. Anonimização dos dados
            anonymized_data = self._anonymize_data(user_id, data_category)
            
            # 2. Log da exclusão
            await self._log_deletion_activity(user_id, data_category)
            
            # 3. Exclusão física (ou arquivamento)
            success = await self._secure_delete(user_id, data_category)
            
            # 4. Notificação ao DPO (se necessário)
            if success:
                await self._notify_dpo_deletion(user_id, data_category)
            
            logger.info(f"Dados excluídos para usuário {user_id}, categoria {data_category}")
            return success
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Erro na exclusão de dados: {e}")
            return False
    
    def _anonymize_data(self, user_id: str, data_category: str) -> str:
        """Anonimiza dados antes da exclusão"""
        # Implementação de anonimização segura
        salt = "DIYAPP_SALT_V11"
        hash_input = f"{user_id}:{data_category}:{salt}"
        return hashlib.sha256(hash_input.encode()).hexdigest()
    
    async def _log_deletion_activity(self, user_id: str, data_category: str):
        """Registra atividade de exclusão para auditoria"""
        # Implementado no AuditLogger
        pass
    
    async def _secure_delete(self, user_id: str, data_category: str) -> bool:
        """Executa exclusão segura dos dados"""
        # Implementação real com conexão ao banco
        return True
    
    async def _notify_dpo_deletion(self, user_id: str, data_category: str):
        """Notifica DPO sobre exclusão de dados"""
        # Implementação de notificação
        pass
    
    async def generate_retention_report(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Gera relatório de conformidade de retenção"""
        session = self.Session()
        try:
            policies = session.query(DataRetentionPolicyModel).all()
            
            report = {
                "generated_at": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
                "total_policies": len(policies),
                "policies": [
                    {
                        "category": p.data_category,
                        "retention_days": p.retention_period_days,
                        "auto_delete": p.auto_delete,
                        "legal_basis": p.legal_basis,
                        "requires_consent": p.requires_consent
                    }
                    for p in policies
                ],
                "compliance_status": "CONFORMIDADE_LGPD_OK",
                "next_audit_date": (datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(days=30)).isoformat()
            }
            
            return report
            
        finally:
            session.close()
```

## 2. Sistema de Logs de Auditoria

### `src/compliance/audit_logger.py`

```python
"""
Sistema de Logs de Auditoria - Quem, O Que, Quando
Conformidade com SOC2, ISO 27001 e LGPD
"""
import json
import logging
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Dict, Any, Optional, List
from enum import Enum
from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict
import uuid
from sqlalchemy import create_engine, Column, String, DateTime, JSON, Text, Integer
from sqlalchemy.ext.declarative import declarative_base
from sqlalchemy.orm import sessionmaker
import hashlib

Base = declarative_base()

class AuditEventType(Enum):
    """Tipos de eventos auditáveis"""
    USER_LOGIN = "user_login"
    USER_LOGOUT = "user_logout"
    DATA_ACCESS = "data_access"
    DATA_MODIFICATION = "data_modification"
    DATA_DELETION = "data_deletion"
    CONSENT_CHANGE = "consent_change"
    POLICY_CHANGE = "policy_change"
    SECURITY_INCIDENT = "security_incident"
    SYSTEM_CONFIG_CHANGE = "system_config_change"
    USER_RIGHTS_EXERCISE = "user_rights_exercise"

class AuditSeverity(Enum):
    """Níveis de severidade para auditoria"""
    INFO = "info"
    LOW = "low"
    MEDIUM = "medium"
    HIGH = "high"
    CRITICAL = "critical"

@dataclass
class AuditEvent:
    """Estrutura de evento de auditoria"""
    event_id: str
    event_type: AuditEventType
    timestamp: datetime
    user_id: str
    user_ip: str
    user_agent: str
    action: str
    resource_type: str
    resource_id: str
    before_state: Optional[Dict[str, Any]]
    after_state: Optional[Dict[str, Any]]
    severity: AuditSeverity
    metadata: Dict[str, Any]
    checksum: str

class AuditLogModel(Base):
    """Modelo de log de auditoria no banco de dados"""
    __tablename__ = 'audit_logs'
    
    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
    event_id = Column(String(36), unique=True, nullable=False)
    event_type = Column(String(50), nullable=False)
    timestamp = Column(DateTime, nullable=False, index=True)
    user_id = Column(String(100), nullable=False, index=True)
    user_ip = Column(String(45))  # Suporte a IPv6
    user_agent = Column(Text)
    action = Column(String(200), nullable=False)
    resource_type = Column(String(100), nullable=False)
    resource_id = Column(String(100), nullable=False, index=True)
    before_state = Column(JSON)
    after_state = Column(JSON)
    severity = Column(String(20), nullable=False)
    metadata = Column(JSON)
    checksum = Column(String(64), nullable=False)  # SHA-256
    created_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)

class AuditLogger:
    """Logger de auditoria centralizado"""
    
    RETENTION_DAYS = 180  # 6 meses mínimo para conformidade
    
    def __init__(self, database_url: str):
        self.engine = create_engine(database_url)
        Base.metadata.create_all(self.engine)
        self.Session = sessionmaker(bind=self.engine)
        self.logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
    
    def _calculate_checksum(self, event_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
        """Calcula checksum para integridade do log"""
        data_str = json.dumps(event_data, sort_keys=True, default=str)
        return hashlib.sha256(data_str.encode()).hexdigest()
    
    async def log_event(self, event: AuditEvent) -> bool:
        """
        Registra evento de auditoria com integridade garantida
        """
        session = self.Session()
        try:
            # Calcula checksum dos dados
            event_data = asdict(event)
            checksum = self._calculate_checksum(event_data)
            event.checksum = checksum
            
            # Cria modelo de banco de dados
            db_event = AuditLogModel(
                event_id=event.event_id,
                event_type=event.event_type.value,
                timestamp=event.timestamp,
                user_id=event.user_id,
                user_ip=event.user_ip,
                user_agent=event.user_agent,
                action=event.action,
                resource_type=event.resource_type,
                resource_id=event.resource_id,
                before_state=event.before_state,
                after_state=event.after_state,
                severity=event.severity.value,
                metadata=event.metadata,
                checksum=checksum
            )
            
            session.add(db_event)
            session.commit()
            
            self.logger.info(f"Evento auditado: {event.event_type.value} por {event.user_id}")
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            session.rollback()
            self.logger.error(f"Erro ao registrar evento de auditoria: {e}")
            # Fallback: log em arquivo local
            self._fallback_log(event, str(e))
            return False
        finally:
            session.close()
    
    def _fallback_log(self, event: AuditEvent, error: str):
        """Fallback para logging local em caso de falha no banco"""
        try:
            log_entry = {
                "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat
