## 2. Sistema de Auditoria (src/compliance/audit_logger.py)

```python
"""
Sistema de Auditoria - Registro de quem, o que, quando
Conformidade com SOC2, ISO 27001 e LGPD
"""
import json
import datetime
import hashlib
from typing import Dict, Any, Optional, List
from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict
from enum import Enum
import sqlite3
from contextlib import contextmanager
import threading

class AuditEventType(Enum):
    """Tipos de eventos auditáveis"""
    USER_LOGIN = "user_login"
    USER_LOGOUT = "user_logout"
    DATA_ACCESS = "data_access"
    DATA_MODIFICATION = "data_modification"
    DATA_DELETION = "data_deletion"
    CONSENT_CHANGE = "consent_change"
    RETENTION_EXECUTION = "retention_execution"
    SECURITY_INCIDENT = "security_incident"
    SYSTEM_CONFIG_CHANGE = "system_config_change"
    USER_RIGHTS_EXERCISE = "user_rights_exercise"
    LLM_INTERACTION = "llm_interaction"

@dataclass
class AuditLogEntry:
    """Entrada de log de auditoria"""
    id: str
    timestamp: datetime.datetime
    event_type: AuditEventType
    user_id: Optional[str]
    user_ip: Optional[str]
    user_agent: Optional[str]
    resource_type: str
    resource_id: str
    action: str
    details: Dict[str, Any]
    success: bool
    metadata: Dict[str, Any]
    
    def to_dict(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Converte para dicionário serializável"""
        data = asdict(self)
        data['event_type'] = self.event_type.value
        data['timestamp'] = self.timestamp.isoformat()
        return data
    
    def to_hash(self) -> str:
        """Gera hash para integridade do log"""
        data_str = json.dumps(self.to_dict(), sort_keys=True)
        return hashlib.sha256(data_str.encode()).hexdigest()

class AuditLogger:
    """Logger de auditoria com garantias de integridade"""
    
    def __init__(self, db_path: str = "audit_logs.db"):
        self.db_path = db_path
        self._init_database()
        self._lock = threading.Lock()
    
    def _init_database(self):
        """Inicializa banco de dados de auditoria"""
        with self._get_connection() as conn:
            conn.execute('''
                CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS audit_logs (
                    id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                    timestamp DATETIME NOT NULL,
                    event_type TEXT NOT NULL,
                    user_id TEXT,
                    user_ip TEXT,
                    user_agent TEXT,
                    resource_type TEXT NOT NULL,
                    resource_id TEXT NOT NULL,
                    action TEXT NOT NULL,
                    details TEXT NOT NULL,
                    success BOOLEAN NOT NULL,
                    metadata TEXT NOT NULL,
                    log_hash TEXT NOT NULL,
                    created_at DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
                )
            ''')
            
            conn.execute('''
                CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_audit_timestamp 
                ON audit_logs(timestamp)
            ''')
            
            conn.execute('''
                CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_audit_user 
                ON audit_logs(user_id)
            ''')
            
            conn.execute('''
                CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_audit_event_type 
                ON audit_logs(event_type)
            ''')
    
    @contextmanager
    def _get_connection(self):
        """Gerencia conexão com banco de dados"""
        conn = sqlite3.connect(self.db_path)
        conn.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
        try:
            yield conn
            conn.commit()
        except Exception:
            conn.rollback()
            raise
        finally:
            conn.close()
    
    def log_event(self, entry: AuditLogEntry) -> bool:
        """
        Registra evento de auditoria com verificação de integridade
        
        Args:
            entry: Entrada de log de auditoria
            
        Returns:
            True se log registrado com sucesso
        """
        with self._lock:
            try:
                entry_dict = entry.to_dict()
                log_hash = entry.to_hash()
                
                with self._get_connection() as conn:
                    conn.execute('''
                        INSERT INTO audit_logs 
                        (id, timestamp, event_type, user_id, user_ip, user_agent,
                         resource_type, resource_id, action, details, success,
                         metadata, log_hash)
                        VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
                    ''', (
                        entry.id,
                        entry_dict['timestamp'],
                        entry_dict['event_type'],
                        entry_dict['user_id'],
                        entry_dict['user_ip'],
                        entry_dict['user_agent'],
                        entry_dict['resource_type'],
                        entry_dict['resource_id'],
                        entry_dict['action'],
                        json.dumps(entry_dict['details']),
                        1 if entry_dict['success'] else 0,
                        json.dumps(entry_dict['metadata']),
                        log_hash
                    ))
                
                # Verificação de integridade pós-inserção
                self._verify_log_integrity(entry.id, log_hash)
                return True
                
            except Exception as e:
                # Fallback: log em arquivo se banco falhar
                self._fallback_log(entry, str(e))
                return False
    
    def _verify_log_integrity(self, log_id: str, expected_hash: str):
        """Verifica integridade do log registrado"""
        with self._get_connection() as conn:
            cursor = conn.execute(
                "SELECT log_hash FROM audit_logs WHERE id = ?",
                (log_id,)
            )
            result = cursor.fetchone()
            
            if result and result['log_hash'] != expected_hash:
                raise ValueError("Integrity check failed for audit log")
    
    def _fallback_log(self, entry: AuditLogEntry, error: str):
        """Fallback para logging em arquivo"""
        log_entry = {
            **entry.to_dict(),
            'fallback': True,
            'db_error': error,
            'fallback_timestamp': datetime.datetime.now().isoformat()
        }
        
        log_file = "audit_fallback.log"
        with open(log_file, 'a') as f:
            f.write(json.dumps(log_entry) + '\n')
    
    def query_logs(self, 
                   start_date: Optional[datetime.datetime] = None,
                   end_date: Optional[datetime.datetime] = None,
                   user_id: Optional[str] = None,
                   event_type: Optional[str] = None,
                   resource_type: Optional[str] = None,
                   limit: int = 1000) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """
        Consulta logs de auditoria com filtros
        
        Args:
            start_date: Data inicial
            end_date: Data final
            user_id: ID do usuário
            event_type: Tipo de evento
            resource_type: Tipo de recurso
            limit: Limite de resultados
            
        Returns:
            Lista de logs de auditoria
        """
        query = "SELECT * FROM audit_logs WHERE 1=1"
        params = []
        
        if start_date:
            query += " AND timestamp >= ?"
            params.append(start_date.isoformat())
        
        if end_date:
            query += " AND timestamp <= ?"
            params.append(end_date.isoformat())
        
        if user_id:
            query += " AND user_id = ?"
            params.append(user_id)
        
        if event_type:
            query += " AND event_type = ?"
            params.append(event_type)
        
        if resource_type:
            query += " AND resource_type = ?"
            params.append(resource_type)
        
        query += " ORDER BY timestamp DESC LIMIT ?"
        params.append(limit)
        
        with self._get_connection() as conn:
            cursor = conn.execute(query, params)
            results = []
            
            for row in cursor.fetchall():
                result = dict(row)
                result['details'] = json.loads(result['details'])
                result['metadata'] = json.loads(result['metadata'])
                results.append(result)
            
            return results
    
    def generate_compliance_report(self, 
                                   period_start: datetime.datetime,
                                   period_end: datetime.datetime) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """
        Gera relatório de conformidade para auditorias
        
        Args:
            period_start: Início do período
            period_end: Fim do período
            
        Returns:
            Relatório de conformidade
        """
        with self._get_connection() as conn:
            # Estatísticas gerais
            cursor = conn.execute('''
                SELECT 
                    COUNT(*) as total_events,
                    COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) as unique_users,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN success = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as successful_events,
                    SUM(CASE WHEN success = 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as failed_events
                FROM audit_logs 
                WHERE timestamp BETWEEN ? AND ?
            ''', (period_start.isoformat(), period_end.isoformat()))
            
            stats = dict(cursor.fetchone())
            
            # Eventos por tipo
            cursor = conn.execute('''
                SELECT event_type, COUNT(*) as count
                FROM audit_logs 
                WHERE timestamp BETWEEN ? AND ?
                GROUP BY event_type
                ORDER BY count DESC
            ''', (period_start.isoformat(), period_end.isoformat()))
            
            events_by_type = [
                {"event_type": row['event_type'], "count": row['count']}
                for row in cursor.fetchall()
            ]
            
            # Usuários mais ativos
            cursor = conn.execute('''
                SELECT user_id, COUNT(*) as activity_count
                FROM audit_logs 
                WHERE timestamp BETWEEN ? AND ? AND user_id IS NOT NULL
                GROUP BY user_id
                ORDER BY activity_count DESC
                LIMIT 10
            ''', (period_start.isoformat(), period_end.isoformat()))
            
            top_users = [
                {"user_id": row['user_id'], "activity_count": row['activity_count']}
                for row in cursor.fetchall()
            ]
            
            # Verificação de integridade
            cursor = conn.execute('''
                SELECT COUNT(*) as total_logs,
                       COUNT(DISTINCT log_hash) as unique_hashes
                FROM audit_logs 
                WHERE timestamp BETWEEN ? AND ?
            ''', (period_start.isoformat(), period_end.isoformat()))
            
            integrity_check = dict(cursor.fetchone())
            integrity_check['integrity_ok'] = (
                integrity_check['total_logs'] == integrity_check['unique_hashes']
            )
            
            return {
                "report_period": {
                    "start": period_start.isoformat(),
                    "end": period_end.isoformat()
                },
                "statistics": stats,
                "events_by_type": events_by_type,
                "top_users": top_users,
                "integrity_check": integrity_check,
                "generated_at": datetime.datetime.now().isoformat(),
                "compliance_standards": ["SOC2", "ISO27001", "LGPD", "GDPR"]
            }
    
    def enforce_retention_policy(self, retention_days: int = 180):
        """
        Aplica política de retenção para logs antigos
        
        Args:
            retention_days: Dias de retenção (padrão 180 para SOC2)
        """
        cutoff_date = datetime.datetime.now() - datetime.timedelta(days=retention_days)
        
        with self._get_connection() as conn:
            # Primeiro arquiva logs que serão excluídos
            self._archive_old_logs(cutoff_date)
            
            # Depois exclui
            conn.execute('''
                DELETE FROM audit_logs 
                WHERE timestamp < ?
            ''', (cutoff_date.isoformat(),))
            
            deleted_count = conn.total_changes
            
            # Log da execução da retenção
            retention_entry = AuditLogEntry(
                id=f"retention_{datetime.datetime.now().timestamp()}",
                timestamp=datetime.datetime.now(),
                event_type=AuditEventType.RETENTION_EXECUTION,
                user_id="system",
                user_ip=None,
                user_agent="retention_policy_enforcer",
                resource_type="audit_logs",
                resource_id="all",
                action="enforce_retention_policy",
                details={
                    "cutoff_date": cutoff_date.isoformat(),
                    "retention_days": retention_days,
                    "deleted_count": deleted_count
                },
                success=True,
                metadata={"compliance_action": True}
            )
            
            self.log_event(retention_entry)
            
            return deleted_count
    
    def _archive_old_logs(self, cutoff_date: datetime.datetime):
        """Arquiva logs antigos antes da exclusão"""
        archive_file = f"audit_archive_{cutoff_date.strftime('%Y%m')}.jsonl"
        
        with self._get_connection() as conn:
            cursor = conn.execute('''
                SELECT * FROM audit_logs 
                WHERE timestamp < ?
                ORDER BY timestamp
            ''', (cutoff_date.isoformat(),))
            
            with open(archive_file, 'w') as f:
                for row in cursor.fetchall():
                    record = dict(row)
                    record['details'] = json.loads(record['details'])
                    record['metadata'] = json.loads(record['metadata'])
                    f.write(json.dumps(record) + '\n')
```

"""
Sistema de Gerenciamento de Consentimento - LGPD/GDPR Compliant
"""
import json
import datetime
from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Set
from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict
from enum import Enum
import sqlite3
import hashlib
from cryptography.fernet import Fernet
import uuid

class ConsentType(Enum):
    """Tipos de consentimento"""
    PRIVACY_POLICY = "privacy_p

### [Sessão Paralela: Compliance]

diyapp-governance/

│   │   ├── migrations/

## 1. Configuração de Políticas de Retenção (LGPD/GDPR Compliant)

### `config/retention_policies.yaml`

```yaml
retention_policies:
  user_account_data:
    data_categories:
      - personal_identification
      - contact_information
      - authentication_data
    retention_period: "730 days"  # 2 anos
    legal_basis: "contract"
    deletion_method: "anonymization"
    exceptions:
      - legal_hold
      - active_dispute
  
  audit_logs:
    data_categories:
      - access_logs
      - action_logs
      - system_events
    retention_period: "180 days"  # 6 meses
    legal_basis: "legal_obligation"
    deletion_method: "secure_deletion"
  
  llm_interactions:
    data_categories:
      - prompts
      - responses
      - metadata
    retention_period: "30 days"
    legal_basis: "legitimate_interest"
    deletion_method: "pseudonymization"
    anonymization_threshold: "immediate"
  
  financial_transactions:
    data_categories:
      - payment_data
      - billing_information
      - tax_records
    retention_period: "1825 days"  # 5 anos
    legal_basis: "legal_obligation"
    deletion_method: "archival"
  
  marketing_consent:
    data_categories:
      - opt_in_records
      - communication_preferences
    retention_period: "365 days after withdrawal"
    legal_basis: "consent"
    deletion_method: "immediate_deletion"

compliance_settings:
  default_region: "BR"
  dpo_email: "dpo@diyapp.com"
  notification_threshold: "72 hours"
  data_subject_response_sla: "15 days"
  breach_assessment_period: "2 hours"
```

### `src/compliance/data_retention.py`

```python
"""
Sistema de Retenção de Dados LGPD/GDPR Compliant
"""
import asyncio
import logging
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import Dict, List, Optional
from enum import Enum
import yaml
from sqlalchemy import create_engine, Column, Integer, String, DateTime, Boolean, JSON
from sqlalchemy.ext.declarative import declarative_base
from sqlalchemy.orm import sessionmaker

Base = declarative_base()

class RetentionPolicy(Base):
    __tablename__ = 'retention_policies'
    
    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
    policy_name = Column(String(100), unique=True, nullable=False)
    data_categories = Column(JSON, nullable=False)
    retention_period_days = Column(Integer, nullable=False)
    legal_basis = Column(String(50), nullable=False)
    deletion_method = Column(String(50), nullable=False)
    is_active = Column(Boolean, default=True)
    created_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow)
    updated_at = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow, onupdate=datetime.utcnow)

class DataRetentionManager:
    """Gerenciador de políticas de retenção LGPD/GDPR"""
    
    def __init__(self, config_path: str = 'config/retention_policies.yaml'):
        self.config = self._load_config(config_path)
        self.logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
        self.engine = None
        self.Session = None
        
    def _load_config(self, config_path: str) -> Dict:
        """Carrega configurações de retenção"""
        try:
            with open(config_path, 'r') as f:
                return yaml.safe_load(f)
        except FileNotFoundError:
            self.logger.warning(f"Config file {config_path} not found, using defaults")
            return self._get_default_config()
    
    def _get_default_config(self) -> Dict:
        """Configurações padrão LGPD compliant"""
        return {
            'retention_policies': {
                'user_account_data': {
                    'retention_period': 730,
                    'legal_basis': 'contract',
                    'deletion_method': 'anonymization'
                },
                'audit_logs': {
                    'retention_period': 180,
                    'legal_basis': 'legal_obligation',
                    'deletion_method': 'secure_deletion'
                }
            }
        }
    
    def initialize_database(self, connection_string: str):
        """Inicializa banco de dados para gestão de retenção"""
        self.engine = create_engine(connection_string)
        Base.metadata.create_all(self.engine)
        self.Session = sessionmaker(bind=self.engine)
        self._load_policies_to_db()
    
    def _load_policies_to_db(self):
        """Carrega políticas do YAML para o banco de dados"""
        session = self.Session()
        try:
            for policy_name, policy_data in self.config.get('retention_policies', {}).items():
                existing = session.query(RetentionPolicy).filter_by(policy_name=policy_name).first()
                if not existing:
                    retention_days = self._parse_retention_period(policy_data.get('retention_period', '30 days'))
                    
                    new_policy = RetentionPolicy(
                        policy_name=policy_name,
                        data_categories=policy_data.get('data_categories', []),
                        retention_period_days=retention_days,
                        legal_basis=policy_data.get('legal_basis', 'legitimate_interest'),
                        deletion_method=policy_data.get('deletion_method', 'secure_deletion')
                    )
                    session.add(new_policy)
            
            session.commit()
            self.logger.info("Retention policies loaded to database")
        except Exception as e:
            session.rollback()
            self.logger.error(f"Error loading policies: {e}")
        finally:
            session.close()
    
    def _parse_retention_period(self, period_str: str) -> int:
        """Converte string de período para dias"""
        try:
            if isinstance(period_str, int):
                return period_str
            
            parts = period_str.split()
            if len(parts) != 2:
                return 30
            
            value = int(parts[0])
            unit = parts[1].lower()
            
            if 'day' in unit:
                return value
            elif 'month' in unit:
                return value * 30
            elif 'year' in unit:
                return value * 365
            else:
                return 30
        except:
            return 30
    
    async def apply_retention_policy(self, table_name: str, data_category: str):
        """Aplica política de retenção a uma tabela específica"""
        session = self.Session()
        try:
            # Encontrar política aplicável
            policy = session.query(RetentionPolicy).filter(
                RetentionPolicy.data_categories.contains([data_category]),
                RetentionPolicy.is_active == True
            ).first()
            
            if not policy:
                self.logger.warning(f"No retention policy found for category: {data_category}")
                return
            
            # Calcular data de corte
            cutoff_date = datetime.utcnow() - timedelta(days=policy.retention_period_days)
            
            # Aplicar método de exclusão baseado na política
            if policy.deletion_method == 'anonymization':
                await self._anonymize_old_data(table_name, cutoff_date)
            elif policy.deletion_method == 'secure_deletion':
                await self._delete_old_data(table_name, cutoff_date)
            elif policy.deletion_method == 'pseudonymization':
                await self._pseudonymize_old_data(table_name, cutoff_date)
            
            self.logger.info(f"Applied {policy.deletion_method} to {table_name} for data older than {cutoff_date}")
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Error applying retention policy: {e}")
        finally:
            session.close()
    
    async def _anonymize_old_data(self, table_name: str, cutoff_date: datetime):
        """Anonimiza dados antigos (LGPD compliant)"""
        # Implementação específica por tabela
        if table_name == 'users':
            query = f"""
            UPDATE {table_name} 
            SET email = CONCAT('anon_', id, '@example.com'),
                name = 'Anonymous User',
                phone = NULL,
                document = NULL,
                anonymized_at = NOW()
            WHERE created_at < %s AND anonymized_at IS NULL
            """
            # Executar query
            pass
    
    async def _delete_old_data(self, table_name: str, cutoff_date: datetime):
        """Exclui dados antigos de forma segura"""
        query = f"DELETE FROM {table_name} WHERE created_at < %s"
        # Executar query com logging de auditoria
        pass
    
    async def _pseudonymize_old_data(self, table_name: str, cutoff_date: datetime):
        """Pseudonimiza dados mantendo referência reversível"""
        # Implementação com chave de criptografia
        pass
    
    def get_retention_schedule(self) -> List[Dict]:
        """Retorna cronograma de execução de retenção"""
        schedule = []
        session = self.Session()
        
        try:
            policies = session.query(RetentionPolicy).filter_by(is_active=True).all()
            
            for policy in policies:
                for category in policy.data_categories:
                    schedule.append({
                        'policy': policy.policy_name,
                        'data_category': category,
                        'retention_days': policy.retention_period_days,
                        'next_execution': self._calculate_next_execution(policy),
                        'legal_basis': policy.legal_basis
                    })
            
            return schedule
        finally:
            session.close()
    
    def _calculate_next_execution(self, policy: RetentionPolicy) -> datetime:
        """Calcula próxima execução baseada na política"""
        # Execução diária para políticas críticas
        return datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(days=1)
```

## 2. Sistema de Auditoria (Quem, O que, Quando)

### `src/compliance/audit_logger.py`

```python
"""
Sistema de Logs de Auditoria LGPD/GDPR Compliant
"""
import json
import logging
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Dict, Any, Optional
from enum import Enum
import hashlib
from sqlalchemy import Column, Integer, String, DateTime, JSON, Text, Index

class AuditAction(Enum):
    """Ações auditáveis no sistema"""
    CREATE = "CREATE"
    READ = "READ"
    UPDATE = "UPDATE"
    DELETE = "DELETE"
    EXPORT = "EXPORT"
    ACCESS = "ACCESS"
    CONSENT_CHANGE = "CONSENT_CHANGE"
    DATA_SUBJECT_REQUEST = "DATA_SUBJECT_REQUEST"
    INCIDENT = "INCIDENT"

class AuditLogger:
    """Logger de auditoria com imutabilidade"""
    
    def __init__(self, db_session):
        self.db = db_session
        self.logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
        
    def log_action(self, 
                   user_id: str,
                   action: AuditAction,
                   resource_type: str,
                   resource_id: str,
                   details: Dict[str, Any],
                   ip_address: Optional[str] = None,
                   user_agent: Optional[str] = None) -> str:
        """Registra ação de auditoria"""
        
        audit_record = {
            'timestamp': datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
            'user_id': user_id,
            'action': action.value,
            'resource_type': resource_type,
            'resource_id': resource_id,
            'details': details,
            'ip_address': ip_address,
            'user_agent': user_agent,
            'checksum': None
        }
        
        # Calcular checksum para integridade
        audit_record['checksum'] = self._calculate_checksum(audit_record)
        
        # Inserir no banco de dados
        try:
            from models.audit_log import AuditLog
            log_entry = AuditLog(
                user_id=user_id,
                action=action.value,
                resource_type=resource_type,
                resource_id=resource_id,
                details=json.dumps(details),
                ip_address=ip_address,
                user_agent=user_agent,
                checksum=audit_record['checksum']
            )
            
            self.db.add(log_entry)
            self.db.commit()
            
            self.logger.info(f"Audit log created: {action.value} on {resource_type}/{resource_id}")
            return log_entry.id
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Failed to create audit log: {e}")
            self.db.rollback()
            raise
    
    def _calculate_checksum(self, record: Dict) -> str:
        """Calcula checksum SHA-256 para integridade do log"""
        # Remover checksum para cálculo
        record_copy = record.copy()
        record_copy.pop('checksum', None)
        
        record_str = json.dumps(record_copy, sort_keys=True)
        return hashlib.sha256(record_str.encode()).hexdigest()
    
    def verify_log_integrity(self, log_id: str) -> bool:
        """Verifica integridade de um log de auditoria"""
        try:
            from models.audit_log import AuditLog
            log_entry = self.db.query(AuditLog).filter_by(id=log_id).first()
            
            if not log_entry:
                return False
            
            # Reconstruir registro
            record = {
                'timestamp': log_entry.timestamp.isoformat(),
                'user_id': log_entry.user_id,
                'action': log_entry.action,
                'resource_type': log_entry.resource_type,
                'resource_id': log_entry.resource_id,
                'details': log_entry.details,
                'ip_address': log_entry.ip_address,
                'user_agent': log_entry.user_agent,
                'checksum': None
            }
            
            # Calcular checksum
            calculated_checksum = self._calculate_checksum(record)
            
            return calculated_checksum == log_entry.checksum
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Error verifying log integrity: {e}")
            return False
    
    def get_audit_trail(self, 
                       resource_type: Optional[str] = None,
                       resource_id: Optional[str] = None,
                       user_id: Optional[str] = None,
                       start_date: Optional[datetime] = None,
                       end_date: Optional[datetime] = None) -> List[Dict]:
        """Recupera trilha de auditoria com filtros"""
        try:
            from models.audit_log import AuditLog
            query = self.db.query(AuditLog)
            
            if resource_type:
                query = query.filter_by(resource_type=resource_type)
            if resource_id:
                query = query.filter_by(resource_id=resource_id)
            if user_id:
                query = query.filter_by(user_id=user_id)
            if start_date:
                query = query.filter(AuditLog.timestamp >= start_date)
            if end_date:
                query = query.filter(AuditLog.timestamp <= end_date)
            
            # Ordenar por timestamp decrescente
            query = query.order_by(AuditLog.timestamp.desc())
            
            logs = query.limit(1000).all()
            
            return [{
                'id': log.id,
                'timestamp': log.timestamp,
                'user_id': log.user_id,
                'action': log.action,
                'resource_type': log.resource_type,
                'resource_id': log.resource_id,
                'details': json.loads(log.details) if log.details else {},
                'ip_address': log.ip_address,
                'user_agent': log.user_agent,
                'integrity_verified': self.verify_log_integrity(log.id)
            } for log in logs]
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Error retrieving audit trail: {e}")
            return []
    
    def generate_compliance_report(self, 
                                  start_date: datetime,
                                  end_date: datetime) -> Dict:
        """Gera relatório de compliance para auditorias"""
        report = {
            'period': {
                'start': start_date.isoformat(),
                'end': end_date.isoformat()
            },
            'summary': {},
            'data_access_logs': [],
            'incidents': [],
            'data_subject_requests': []
        }
        
        # Coletar estatísticas
        from models.audit_log import AuditLog
        from sqlalchemy import func
        
        try:
            # Contagem por ação
            action_counts = self.db.query(
                AuditLog.action,
                func.count(AuditLog.id)
            ).filter(
                AuditLog.timestamp.between(start_date, end_date)
